中文摘要：基于任务的聊天机器人如今被广泛采用，通常集成到实际应用和通信渠道中，旨在通过对话界面协助用户完成任务。与其他软件一样，聊天机器人也容易出现错误。尽管它们在日常活动中日益普及，但现有的评估其质量的技术仍然存在一些局限性，例如生成的测试场景过于简单以及预言弱点。在本文中，我们提出了LexTester，一种针对Amazon Lex聊天机器人的自动化基于模型的测试技术。该技术探索被测聊天机器人的对话空间，生成所有可能交互的对话图，然后根据不同的覆盖策略从中生成可执行的测试套件。我们在五个Amazon Lex聊天机器人上将LexTester与最先进的聊天机器人测试工具Botium进行了评估，LexTester在所有测试对象上均持续优于Botium，生成了更多测试，复杂度几乎翻倍，对话元素覆盖率达到83-95%，错误检测有效性提高了高达四倍，而时间成本相当。

Original abstract: Task-based chatbots are nowadays widely adopted software systems, usually integrated into real-world applications and communication channels, designed to assist users in completing tasks through conversational interfaces. Like any other software, even chatbots are prone to bugs. Despite their increasing pervasiveness in everyday activities, existing techniques for assessing their quality still exhibit several limitations, such as the simplicity of generated test scenarios and oracle weaknesses.
  In this paper, we present LexTester, an automated model-based testing technique for Amazon Lex chatbots. The technique explores the conversational space of the chatbot under test to generate a Dialog Graph of all possible interactions, from which an executable test suite is generated according to different coverage strategies. LexTester was evaluated against the state-of-the-practice chatbot testing tool Botium on five Amazon Lex chatbots, consistently outperforming it in all subjects, generating more tests with nearly double complexity, achieving overall 83-95% coverage of conversational elements, and improving fault detection effectiveness by up to four times at comparable time costs.

*Tyler Sivertsen,Neal Singh,James C. Davis*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: SAGE是一个基于浏览器的工具，通过自然语言提示引导编辑工程图表，将图结构、XML修复和版本控制集成在一个系统中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自然语言编辑软件图表需要同时保留视觉布局、结构和语义关系，现有工具难以做到。

Method: 将图表映射为图表示，自然语言请求转换为结构化编辑意图，分析为图操作步骤，验证修复XML，支持直接画布和蒙版编辑。

Original abstract: Software diagrams are difficult to edit through human-friendly interfaces because edits expressed in natural language must still preserve visual layout, editable structure, and semantic relationships. As a step forward, we present SAGE, a browser-based tool for prompt-guided editing of Draw.io and Mermaid-style engineering diagrams. The tool maps diagrams into an editable graph representation, translates natural language requests into structured edit intents, analyzes those intents into graph-oriented operation steps, validates and repairs common Draw.io XML issues, and stores successful results as recoverable versioned artifacts. This design separates structured state management from model-driven interpretation, while acknowledging that some prompt-guided XML edits remain model-assisted. The tool also supports direct canvas editing and a secondary mask-based image-editing workflow. We evaluate the system using unit tests and a Kubernetes architecture case study, measuring structural validity, edit success, preservation of unrelated elements, and failure causes.

### [34] [Skills Are Not Islands: Measuring Dependency and Risk in Agent Skill Supply Chains](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01136v1)
*Changguo Jia,Tianqi Zhao,Runzhi He,Minghui Zhou*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 针对LLM智能体技能依赖管理缺失的问题，提出ASSCs和SkillDepAnalyzer，在143万技能中揭示了依赖图结构模式和安全信号，并给出改进建议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM智能体技能包缺乏有效的依赖管理，导致重复安装和版本不一致，亟需系统化的依赖建模与分析工具。

Method: 借鉴软件物料清单（SBOM）思想，设计SkillDepAnalyzer，利用自然语言处理提取技能依赖证据，构建混合依赖图（ASSCs），并在大规模技能库上进行分析。

Result: SkillDepAnalyzer在SKILL-DEP基准上准确恢复依赖图，优于基线；应用于143万技能发现四种结构模式，并识别出持续存在的恶意技能。

Conclusion: 建议采用类型化依赖清单、依赖集群管理、风险审计命令和锁文件机制，以提升技能依赖的透明性和安全性。

中文摘要：智能体技能包将可复用的操作知识打包用于大语言模型智能体，然而随着其范围的扩大，它们变成了具有依赖关系的工件，其身份、版本和来源仍然不明确。这种不透明性已经导致重复的依赖项和不一致的安装，暴露出依赖管理尚未填补的空白。我们引入了智能体技能供应链（ASSCs）来描述混合的技能-包-服务依赖图并帮助填补这一空白。借鉴软件物料清单（SBOMs），我们设计了SkillDepAnalyzer来捕获自然语言依赖证据，并将技能建模为具有依赖关系的工件。在SKILL-DEP基准上，SkillDepAnalyzer准确且全面地恢复了技能元数据和依赖图，显著优于基于LLM的基线和以包为中心的SBOM工具。将SkillDepAnalyzer应用于超过143万个技能，我们获得了ASSCs并探索了它们的结构多样性和安全信号。我们发现了四种结构模式：技能元数据可随时激活但治理薄弱；依赖图涵盖技能、包和服务依赖，且具有集中的复用性；递归的技能复用扩展依赖图并产生隐藏的包库存；技能依赖集群围绕相关工作流形成。我们还发现仅检查单个技能会遗漏隐藏在其依赖项中的安全相关信号。通过分析ASSCs，我们识别并向其开发者报告了持续存在ASSCs中的已知恶意技能。基于这些发现，我们建议技能基础设施维护者使用类型化依赖清单、一级依赖集群管理、风险警告审计命令，以及技能开发者使用类似锁文件的记录。

Original abstract: Agent skills package reusable operational knowledge for Large Language Model (LLM) agents, yet as they grow in scope, they become dependency-bearing artifacts whose identities, versions, and provenance remain implicit. This opacity already causes duplicated dependencies and inconsistent installations, exposing a gap that dependency management has yet to close. We introduce Agent Skill Supply Chains (ASSCs) to characterize mixed skill-package-service dependency graphs and help close this gap. Borrowing from Software Bill of Materials (SBOMs), we design SkillDepAnalyzer to capture natural-language dependency evidence and model skills as dependency-bearing artifacts. On the SKILL-DEP benchmark, SkillDepAnalyzer recovers skill metadata and dependency graphs accurately and comprehensively, substantially outperforming an LLM-based baseline and package-centric SBOM tools. Applying SkillDepAnalyzer to over 1.43 million skills, we obtain ASSCs and explore their structural diversity and security signals. We find four structural patterns: skill metadata is activation-ready but governance-poor; dependency graphs span skill, package, and service dependencies with concentrated reuse; recursive skill reuse expands dependency graphs and creates hidden package inventory; and skill dependency clusters form around related workflows. We also find that inspecting a skill alone misses security-relevant signals hiding in its dependencies. By analyzing ASSCs, we identify and report known malicious skills persisting in ASSCs to their developers. Based on these findings, we recommend typed dependency manifests, first-class dependency-cluster management, risk-warning audit commands for skill infrastructure maintainers, and lockfile-like records for skill developers.

</details>


### [35] [Are Performance-Optimization Benchmarks Reliably Measuring Coding Agents?](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01211v2)
*Zhi Chen,Zhensu Sun,Yuling Shi,David Lo,Lingxiao Jiang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 对GSO、SWE-Perf和SWE-fficiency三个仓库级性能优化基准的审计表明，大多数参考补丁存在跨机器可重复性问题，评分规则导致排名不一致，且大量任务已被公开提交解决，揭示了排行榜分数的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 排行榜分数常被用作编码代理进展的证据，但这些分数可能因运行时不稳定、评分规则差异和任务已被解决而失真，需要进行系统性审计以揭示真实性能。

Method: 重放740个任务的官方参考补丁于四种Google Cloud机器上验证有效性；对比八个公开提交的评分规则一致性；分析每个任务多个提交的表现。

Result: 仅少数参考补丁跨机器有效（GSO 38%，SWE-Perf 8%，SWE-fficiency 83%）；评分规则导致排名分歧；大部分任务已有至少一个提交达到或超过参考补丁（85.3%）。

Conclusion: 当前基准的排行榜分数不可靠，需结合任务级可靠信号、分数权重和剩余性能差距来综合评估编码代理进展。

中文摘要：仓库级性能优化基准测试（如GSO、SWE-Perf和SWE-fficiency）通过将补丁应用于真实仓库并对比运行时间与未优化基线和官方参考补丁来评估编码代理。其排行榜分数越来越多地被用作编码代理进展的证据，但这些分数可能混淆运行时不稳定、基准特定评分规则以及有多少任务已被至少一个公开提交解决。我们对这三个基准的这些问题进行了审计。首先，我们在四种常见的Google Cloud机器类型上重放了740个代码优化任务的官方参考补丁。大多数基准任务可以重放，但它们的参考补丁在所有跨机器重放中满足原始基准有效性规则的只有39/102的GSO任务、11/140的SWE-Perf任务和411/498的SWE-fficiency任务；SWE-Perf尤其脆弱，因为许多参考补丁产生的运行时变化几乎为零。其次，我们显示公开提交排名在很大程度上取决于基准评分规则。在GSO和SWE-fficiency共享的八个公开提交中，官方排名在28对提交比较中有9对不一致，而SWE-fficiency的排行榜评分规则将最差的十个任务的分数权重分配过高，达到58.5%-82.8%。第三，观察每个任务的10个公开提交，我们发现至少有1个提交在85.3%（384/450）的可重放GSO和SWE-fficiency任务中达到或超过了参考补丁，在99.8%（449/450）的任务中击败了未优化的基础代码。我们的研究通过识别具有更可靠性能信号的任务、量化每个任务的分数贡献以及揭示被聚合排名隐藏的剩余性能差距，补充了排行榜分数。

Original abstract: Repository-level performance-optimization benchmarks such as GSO, SWE-Perf and SWE-fficiency evaluate coding agents by applying patches to real repositories and comparing runtime against unoptimized baselines and official reference patches. Their leaderboard scores are increasingly used as evidence of coding-agent progress, but those scores can conflate runtime instability, benchmark-specific scoring rules, and how many tasks are already solved by at least one public submission. We audit these issues across the three benchmarks. First, we replay the official reference patches for 740 code optimization tasks across four common types of Google Cloud machines. Most benchmark tasks can be replayed, but their reference patches satisfy the original benchmark validity rules in every cross-machine replay for only 39/102 GSO tasks, 11/140 SWE-Perf tasks, and 411/498 SWE-fficiency tasks; SWE-Perf is especially fragile because many reference patches produce close-to-zero runtime changes. Second, we show that public submission rankings depend strongly on the benchmark scoring rule. Among eight public submissions shared by GSO and SWE-fficiency, the official rankings disagree on 9 of 28 pairwise submission comparisons, and SWE-fficiency's leaderboard scoring rule assigns the worst ten tasks overly high score weights of 58.5%-82.8%. Third, looking across 10 public submissions for each task, we find that at least one submission matches or beats the reference patch on 85.3% (384/450) of replay-valid GSO and SWE-fficiency tasks, and beats the unoptimized base code on 99.8% (449/450). Our study complements leaderboard scores by identifying tasks with more reliable performance signals, quantifying per-task score contributions, and exposing the remaining performance gaps that are hidden by aggregate rankings.

</details>


### [36] [RepoRescue: An Empirical Study of LLM Agents on Whole-Repository Compatibility Rescue](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01213v1)
*Zhihao Lin,Mingyi Zhou,Zhensu Sun,Yizhuo Yang,Renyu Yang,David Lo,Li Li*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: LLM智能体在兼容性救援任务中的表现评估，发现系统互补且跨文件协调是主要难点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着开源项目维护者离开，仓库可能因环境演化而失效，需要自动适应现代环境。

Method: 构建了包含193个Python和122个Java仓库的基准测试RepoRescue，评估多个LLM智能体系统，包括仅源代码修复、运行时强制和实际验证等指标。

Result: Claude Code系统会编辑测试文件，但通过运行时阻塞后Kimi救援率41.5%；系统联合通过率62.7%；跨文件协调是难点，GPT-5.2通过率100%。

Conclusion: 兼容性救援可行但系统存在互补性，需要进一步改进跨文件协调能力。

中文摘要：开源库和工具被广泛复用，但兼容性维护成本高昂。一旦维护者离开，随着运行时和依赖项的演化，有用的仓库可能会停止工作。我们研究LLM智能体是否能够使老旧仓库适应现代环境，我们将此任务称为兼容性救援。与错误修复不同，兼容性救援从一个在原始环境中正常工作但生态系统漂移后失败的仓库开始。RepoRescue仅向智能体提供仓库及其失败的现代环境；智能体必须诊断失败原因、定位受影响的代码，并生成恢复历史测试套件的源代码救援方案。我们从193个Python仓库和122个Java仓库构建了RepoRescue，每个仓库都经过验证，历史上能通过测试但在现代化后失败。我们对Python上的五个已部署智能体系统和Java上的三个系统进行了评估。除了完整补丁通过率，我们还在移除测试文件编辑后重新运行补丁以测量仅源代码修复，添加了运行时强制机制来阻止测试编辑，并验证了仓库在救援后测试套件通过的实际使用情况。我们发现Claude Code系统有时会在被提示不要修改时仍编辑失败的测试；在运行时阻塞下，Kimi仍然能救援41.5%的仓库。系统具有互补性：它们的联合通过率达到62.7%，超过最佳单一系统10.9个百分点。困难集中在跨文件协调上：在需要全代码库协调修改的14个仓库中，GPT-5.2通过Codex通过了全部14个，而每个Claude Code系统最多通过两个。最后，通过测试套件只是一个初始信号：在34个无人维护的Python候选仓库中，其测试套件在救援后通过，其中22个在现实场景中有效，12个通过了补丁能解决兼容性故障的漏洞狩猎。RepoRescue通过仅源代码审计、运行时强制、实际验证和推理标签对兼容性救援进行了基准测试。

Original abstract: Open-source libraries and tools are widely reused, but compatibility maintenance is expensive. Once maintainers leave, useful repositories can stop working as runtimes and dependencies evolve. We study whether LLM agents can adapt old repositories to modern environments, a task we call compatibility rescue. Unlike bug repair, compatibility rescue starts from a repository that worked in its original environment but fails after ecosystem drift. RepoRescue gives agents only the repository and its failing modern environment; the agent must diagnose the failure, locate affected code, and produce a source-code rescue that restores the historical test suite. We build RepoRescue from 193 Python and 122 Java repositories, each verified to pass historically and fail after modernization. We evaluate five deployed agent systems on Python and three on Java. Beyond full-patch pass rate, we rerun patches after removing test-file edits to measure source-only repair, add a runtime-enforced regime that blocks test edits, and validate practical use for repositories whose suites pass after rescue. We find that Claude Code systems sometimes edit failing tests even when prompted not to; with runtime blocking, Kimi still rescues 41.5% of repositories. Systems are complementary: their union reaches 62.7%, exceeding the best single system by 10.9 points. Difficulty concentrates in cross-file coordination: on 14 repositories requiring coordinated whole-codebase changes, GPT-5.2 through Codex passes all 14, while every Claude Code system passes at most two. Finally, a passing suite is only an initial signal: among 34 unmaintained Python candidates whose suites pass after rescue, 22 work in realistic scenarios and 12 pass bug-hunt with patches that address the compatibility failure. RepoRescue benchmarks compatibility rescue with source-only auditing, runtime enforcement, practical validation, and reasoning labels.

</details>


### [37] [Benchmarking Code Improvement with Progressive, Adaptive, and Interactive Feedback](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01360v1)
*Cuong Chi Le,Aashish Yadavally,Minh Le-Anh,Tien N. Nguyen*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: PAIR-Bench是一个用于评估LLM代码改进能力的基准，通过渐进式提示和结构化反馈来细化评估，比简单的二进制通过/失败更细致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估仅基于二进制功能正确性，忽略了部分进展、反馈利用和细化轨迹，无法全面衡量LLM的代码改进能力。

Method: 设计PAIR-Bench，包含渐进式提示协议，通过失败区域控制和提示深度控制两个维度提供结构化反馈，并评估修复轨迹的多个方面。

Result: PAIR-Bench能够更细粒度地评估模型是否修复目标失败、泛化、保持正确行为以及所需帮助程度。

Conclusion: PAIR-Bench通过渐进式指标提供了对LLM代码改进能力的更全面评估，优于仅通过/失败的方法。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）通常在代码生成和程序修复中使用二元功能正确性进行评估：生成的程序或补丁要么通过要么失败测试套件。这种协议简单但粗糙，因为它忽略了部分进展、反馈利用、回归以及模型通常通过改进代码的细化轨迹。我们引入了PAIR-Bench，一个用于评估代码改进的渐进式和自适应基准：通过反馈引导的细化将不正确或不完整的程序转变为更正确的程序。PAIR-Bench使用渐进式提示，一种具有两个控制的结构化反馈协议。失败区域控制通过将隐藏的失败测试分组为失败场景来确定反馈的目标，而提示深度控制控制揭示多少与修复相关的信息，从粗略症状到实现级指导。这种设计使PAIR-Bench能够衡量模型是否修复了目标失败、是否超越了提示进行泛化、是否保持了已经正确的行为，以及它需要多少帮助。通过评估修复轨迹的渐进式指标，而不仅仅是最终的通过/失败结果，PAIR-Bench提供了对LLM代码改进能力的更细粒度评估。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are typically evaluated on code generation and program repair using binary functional correctness: a generated program or patch either passes or fails a test suite. This protocol is simple but coarse, as it ignores partial progress, feedback use, regressions, and the refinement trajectory through which models often improve code. We introduce PAIR-Bench, a progressive and adaptive benchmark for evaluating code improvement: transforming an incorrect or incomplete program into a more correct one through feedback-guided refinement. PAIR-Bench uses progressive hinting, a structured feedback protocol with two controls. Failure-region control determines what the feedback targets by grouping hidden failing tests into failure scenarios, while hint-depth control determines how much repair-relevant information is revealed, from coarse symptoms to implementation-level guidance. This design enables PAIR-Bench to measure whether a model repairs targeted failures, generalizes beyond the hint, preserves already-correct behavior, and how much assistance it requires. By evaluating repair trajectories progressive metrics rather than only final pass/fail outcomes, PAIR-Bench provides a finer-grained assessment of LLM code-improvement capability.

</details>


### [38] [A global predicted-fMRI drive signal from TRIBE does not predict YouTube replay heatmaps](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01400v2)
*Barada Sahu,Shivesh Pandey*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: TRIBE模型预测的神经信号不能预测YouTube视频的观看重播行为，多种分析均支持零结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究深度脑编码模型预测的fMRI响应是否能进一步预测自然视频观看中的行为参与（如重播指标）。

Method: 将TRIBE模型应用于48个YouTube视频，提取预测的全局场功率作为每秒参与度曲线，与YouTube“最重播”热力图进行位置控制偏相关、置换检验、监督探针、输入流分拆分析，并自建被试间相关性模型进行验证。

Result: 所有分析均未发现显著预测能力：偏相关r=0.058（p=0.23），贝叶斯因子BF01=3.2，等价检验排除r>0.14，监督探针在位置控制下崩塌，输入流仅视觉有边缘信号，预测ISC不跟踪重播（r=-0.04）。

Conclusion: 尽管脑编码模型能高精度预测神经响应，但其预测信号不能预测行为参与，未来工作需探索更好的行为预测指标或模型。

中文摘要：深度多模态脑编码模型现在能够高精度地预测对自然视频的fMRI响应；但它们的预测神经信号是否也能预测行为参与尚不清楚。我们将TRIBE（2025年Algonauts挑战赛的获胜模型，Llama-3.2 + V-JEPA 2 + Wav2Vec-BERT）应用于48个YouTube视频，并将其预测的皮层响应缩减为每秒参与度曲线，即全局场功率。与每个视频的“最重播”热力图（重看的代理指标）进行相关性分析，结果显示没有预测证据：合并的位置控制偏相关为+0.058（95% CI [-0.04, 0.15]；t(47)=1.21，p=0.23），且不低于简单的响度/运动基线。原始相关性也接近零；音乐视频的适度值是一个起始重放伪影。零假设在六个皮层网络读数、价值/显著性ROI和置换检验中均成立；一个监督的留一视频外推断探针似乎达到r=0.47，但在适当的位置控制下崩塌为时间形状伪影。在TRIBE的输入流上运行该探针，最多显示一个微小、边缘性的视觉流信号（匹配与不匹配p=0.004-0.06），而在音频、文本或预测皮层中则没有。最接近先前阳性结果的被试间相关性读数，无法从被试平均的发布模型中获得，因此我们自己在Algonauts fMRI上拟合了每个被试的编码器（域内验证r=0.15，跨域Friends到电影r=0.10）；预测的ISC仍然不跟踪重播（r=-0.04，p=0.34）。我们界限而非仅仅无法拒绝零假设：贝叶斯因子提供中等证据支持零假设（BF01=3.2），等价检验排除效应大于r=0.14，目标的分半信度（0.82；上限r=0.9）排除了噪声标签伪影。我们发布代码、视频ID清单和一种对YouTube的SABR流稳健的热力图获取方法。

Original abstract: Deep multimodal brain-encoding models now predict fMRI responses to naturalistic video with high accuracy; whether their predicted neural signals also forecast behavioral engagement is unknown. We run TRIBE, the winning model of the 2025 Algonauts challenge (Llama-3.2 + V-JEPA 2 + Wav2Vec-BERT), on 48 YouTube videos and reduce its predicted cortical response to a per-second engagement curve, the global field power. Correlated against each video's "most replayed" heatmap, a proxy for re-watch, it shows no evidence of prediction: the pooled position-controlled partial correlation is +0.058 (95% CI [-0.04, 0.15]; t(47)=1.21, p=0.23), and not above simple loudness/motion baselines. The raw correlation is also near zero; the moderate values for music videos are an onset-replay artifact. The null holds across six cortical-network readouts, value/salience ROIs, and a permutation test; a supervised leave-one-video-out probe appears to reach r=0.47 but collapses to a temporal-shape artifact under a proper position control. Running the probe on TRIBE's input streams reveals at most a small, borderline visual-stream signal (matched vs. mismatched p=0.004-0.06) and none in audio, text, or the predicted cortex. The inter-subject-correlation readout, the closest prior positive result, is unavailable from the subject-averaged released model, so we fit our own per-subject encoders on the Algonauts fMRI (validated in-domain at r=0.15 and cross-domain, Friends-to-film, at r=0.10); the predicted ISC still does not track re-watch (r=-0.04, p=0.34). We bound rather than merely fail to reject the null: a Bayes factor gives moderate evidence for it (BF01=3.2), an equivalence test excludes effects above r=0.14, and the target's split-half reliability (0.82; ceiling r=0.9) rules out a noisy-label artifact. We release code, a video-ID manifest, and a heatmap-acquisition method robust to YouTube's SABR streaming.

</details>


### [39] [GPUAlert: A Zero-Instrumentation Process-Boundary Monitor for Diagnosing GPU Training-Job Failures](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01409v1)
*Parv Agarwal,Asif Ekbal*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: GPUAlert是一个无需修改训练脚本的命令行包装器，能在训练完成时发送结构化电子邮件通知，并通过三个可靠性原语实现低开销和可靠监控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GPU训练任务频繁失败且故障检测延迟大，现有方案（实验跟踪器、调度器邮件钩子）存在需要修改脚本、依赖云连接或信息不足等问题。

Method: 设计命令行包装器GPUAlert，包含三个可靠性原语（启动前日志保证、通知隔离、非静默工件预算），并构建含474个日志和15个失败类别的语料库，使用有序规则分类器进行故障分类。

Result: 有序规则分类器在12个硬件可重现类别上达到0.997宏F1，远优于无序关键词匹配（0.830）和退出码检查（0.133）；包装器开销约3ms/任务，启动前日志保证有效，SMTP不可达时仍返回正确退出码。

Conclusion: GPUAlert能够以极低开销和无需修改脚本的方式实现高精度的故障分类和可靠的通知，有效解决了训练任务失败检测和诊断的问题。

中文摘要：GPU训练任务经常失败，在大型生产集群上大约五分之二会失败，然而操作员通常只有在数小时后重新连接时才会得知失败。实验跟踪器需要编辑训练脚本并保持云连接；调度器的邮件钩子只发送一行状态信息，没有原因和日志。GPUAlert是一个命令行包装器，在进程边界监控任何训练命令，且无需对该命令进行修改，在完成时通过电子邮件发送结构化通知，其中包含分类后的失败原因、持久化日志和输出工件。该工具围绕三个可靠性原语组织：启动前日志保证，在子进程可能崩溃之前建立持久化目的地；通知隔离，使得包装器的退出码成为子进程状态的纯函数，无论邮件是否成功发送；以及非静默工件预算，限制附件大小而不静默丢弃输出。我们发布了一个包含474个GPU训练日志、涵盖15个失败类别的带标注语料库，以及一个可重现的评估框架。在十二个硬件可重现的类别上，有序规则分类器达到0.997的宏平均F1，而无序关键词匹配为0.830，退出码检查为0.133。每个作业的包装器开销恒定约为3毫秒；启动前保证在shell重定向不产生任何内容时仍保留日志；在所有15种失败模式下，即使SMTP中继不可达，包装器返回的子进程退出码也保持不变。

Original abstract: GPU training jobs fail often, roughly two in five on large production clusters, yet the operator typically learns of a failure only by reconnecting hours later. Experiment trackers require editing the training script and maintaining a cloud connection; the scheduler's mail hook delivers a single status line with no cause and no logs. GPUAlert is a command-line wrapper that monitors any training command at the process boundary, and with no change to that command, emails a structured notification on completion carrying a classified failure cause, durable logs, and output artifacts. The tool is organized around three reliability primitives: a pre-launch log guarantee that establishes the durable destination before the child process can crash, notifier isolation that makes the wrapper's exit code a pure function of the child's status regardless of whether the email succeeds, and a non-silent artifact budget that bounds attachment size without ever dropping output silently. We release a labelled corpus of 474 GPU training logs across 15 failure classes and a reproducible evaluation harness. On the twelve hardware-reproduced classes, the ordered-rule classifier reaches 0.997 macro-F1, against 0.830 for unordered keyword matching and 0.133 for exit-code inspection. Wrapper overhead is a constant approximately 3ms per job; the pre-launch guarantee preserves a log where a shell redirect yields nothing; and across all 15 failure modes the wrapper returns the child's exit code unchanged even when the SMTP relay is unreachable.

### [40] [Adoption and Impact of Command-Line AI Coding Agents: A Study of Microsoft's Early 2026 Rollout of Claude Code and GitHub Copilot CLI](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01418v1)
*Emerson Murphy-Hill,Jenna Butler,Alexandra Savelieva*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 微软早期推广CLI编码代理的研究发现，首次使用通过社交网络传播，留存与编码活动相关，采用者PR合并量增加约24%，表明工具并非新奇效应，推广应聚焦同行可见使用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 组织需要了解代理命令行工具（如Claude Code、Copilot CLI）的采用模式、留存因素和产出影响，以避免高昂的推广成本却未改变工程速度。

Method: 在微软2026年初的推广中，对数万名工程师进行研究，分析社交网络传播、留存与编码活动/人口统计学的关系，并采用差分方法评估对PR合并量的影响。

Result: 首次使用主要通过社交网络传播；留存与编码活动相关而非人口统计学；采用者合并PR量增加约24%且效果持续四个月。

Conclusion: CLI编码代理并非统一采用或短暂新奇效应，组织应将可见的同行使用作为推广策略的核心。

中文摘要：正在推出像Anthropic的Claude Code和GitHub的Copilot CLI这样的代理命令行工具的组织需要知道谁会尝试它们，谁会继续使用它们，以及这些工具是否产生足够的输出来证明其成本。在组织规模上，代币支出每年可能高达数百万美元，因此对采用、留存或影响的误判可能使推广成本高昂而不会改变工程速度。通过在微软2026年初的推广中研究数万名工程师，我们发现首次使用主要通过社交网络传播，留存与工程师的编码活动的关联大于与人口统计学的关联，并且采用者合并的拉取请求比原本多大约24%。我们使用合并的拉取请求作为输出的代理——承认合并的PR并不等同于其交付的价值——并且这种提升在我们的四个月窗口期内持续存在。这些结果表明，CLI编码代理既没有被统一采用，也不是单纯的新奇效应，组织应将可见的同行使用视为推广策略的核心。

Original abstract: Organizations rolling out agentic command line tools like Anthropic's Claude Code and GitHub's Copilot CLI need to know who will try them, who will keep using them, and whether the tools produce enough output to justify their cost. At organizational scale, token spend can run into millions of dollars annually, so misreading adoption, retention, or impact can make a rollout expensive without changing engineering velocity. Studying tens of thousands of engineers at Microsoft over its early-2026 rollout, we find that first use spread primarily through social networks, retention was associated more with engineers' coding activity than with demographics, and adopters merged roughly 24% more pull requests than they would have otherwise. We use merged pull requests as our proxy for output -- acknowledging that a merged PR is not the same as the value it delivers -- and the lift persists across our four-month window. These results suggest that CLI coding agents are neither uniformly adopted nor mere novelty effects and that organizations should treat visible peer use as central to rollout strategy.

</details>


### [41] [Risk Architecture for AI-Native Engineering Teams: An Organizational Framework for Agentic System Governance](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01421v1)
*Laxmipriya Ganesh Iyer*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出了区分软件团队类型的七维度概况、六聚类故障模式分类法，以及评估风险框架充分性的方法论，发现从纯软件工程到AI原生团队过渡时，覆盖率下降且最严重故障出现在组织边界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有软件风险管理框架基于确定性假设，不适用于代理型AI系统；而AI风险文献未关注工程经理层面的角色和决策权，因此需要新的框架评估方法。

Method: 通过定义七维度团队概况和六聚类故障模式分类，提出综合框架充分性方法论，对每个概况的风险架构进行场景集评估。

Result: 覆盖率随团队从纯软件工程向AI原生过渡而下降，中位数单调递减，且AI原生步骤中出现大量未覆盖的高后果故障；最严重故障出现在组织边界而非AI原生团队内部。

Conclusion: 现有风险框架在AI原生场景下严重不足，特别是依赖边界确定性不匹配导致的高后果故障未被覆盖，需针对工程管理层面重新设计风险架构。

中文摘要：工程管理研究已经产生了成熟的软件风险框架：按功能划分所有权、按严重程度升级、按测试覆盖率保障。这些框架隐含地假设确定性行为、离散且可审计的变更事件，以及清晰的组件到所有者映射。构建和运营代理型AI系统的团队同时违反了所有三个假设：输出是概率性的，系统自主采取多步骤行动，风险面在部署之间静默变化。现有的AI风险文献从上层（如NIST AI RMF和ISO/IEC 42001等政策框架）或下层（如OWASP代理型AI指南等威胁分类法）进行处理，但并未涉及工程经理（EM）操作层面：角色、决策权和升级结构。本文贡献了：(i)一个七维度的概况，区分纯软件工程、混合和AI原生团队；(ii)一个六聚类的故障模式分类法，包括一个之前未阐明的聚类——依赖边界确定性不匹配；(iii)一个综合框架充分性方法论，评估每个概况的风险架构对定义场景集的检测、遏制和升级能力。由于研究对象是框架充分性而非人类行为，评估得出的是推导性而非观察性的覆盖声明。随着团队从纯软件工程过渡到AI原生运营，覆盖率下降，中位数单调递减，而在AI原生步骤中突然出现大量未覆盖的高后果故障。退化集中在特定的故障模式类别中，最严重、覆盖最少的故障并非出现在AI原生团队内部，而是在组织边界，其中他们的概率性输出被假设确定性的依赖方所消费。

Original abstract: Engineering management research has produced mature frameworks for software risk: ownership by feature, escalation by severity, and assurance by test coverage. These frameworks implicitly assume deterministic behavior, discrete and auditable change events, and clear component-to-owner mappings. Teams that build and operate agentic AI systems violate all three assumptions at once: outputs are probabilistic, systems take autonomous multi-step actions, and the risk surface mutates silently between deployments. Existing AI risk literature addresses this from above (policy frameworks such as the NIST AI RMF and ISO/IEC 42001) or below (threat taxonomies such as OWASP's agentic AI guidance), but not at the layer where an engineering manager (EM) operates: roles, decision rights, and escalation structures. This paper contributes (i) a seven-dimension profile distinguishing pure software-engineering, hybrid, and AI-native teams; (ii) a six-cluster failure-mode taxonomy including a previously unarticulated cluster, dependency-boundary determinism mismatch; and (iii) a synthetic framework-adequacy methodology scoring how well each profile's risk architecture detects, contains, and escalates a defined scenario set. Because the object of study is framework adequacy rather than human behavior, the evaluation yields derived rather than observed coverage claims. Coverage degrades as teams move from pure software engineering to AI-native operation, monotonically in the median and abruptly in the count of uncovered, high-consequence failures appearing only at the AI-native step. The degradation concentrates in specific failure-mode categories, and the most severe, least-covered failures arise not inside AI-native teams but at the organizational boundary where their probabilistic outputs are consumed by determinism-assuming dependencies.

</details>


### [42] [From Anatomy to Smells: An Empirical Study of SKILL.md in Agent Skills](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01456v2)
*David Boram Hong,Aaron Imani,Iftekhar Ahmed*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 首次系统研究Agent Skill的SKILL$.$md文件，发现超过99%的文件存在技能异味，且很少消失，表明编写实践与推荐实践严重脱节。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Agent Skills被广泛采用，但SKILL$.$md文件的编写实践缺乏系统研究，现有指南是否被遵循未知，因此需要系统了解实际编写情况与最佳实践之间的差距。

Method: 定性分析238个真实技能推导语义分类，多声部文献综述29个来源提取最佳实践并定义技能异味，开发自动检测器应用于真实技能。

Result: 超过99%的SKILL$.$md文件至少含有一个技能异味，且技能异味在演化中很少消失。

Conclusion: 推荐实践与实际编写实践存在显著差距，需开发自动化工具修复技能异味，并提高开发者对质量问题的认识。

中文摘要：Agent Skills为LLM代理提供按需领域知识，无需模型重新训练。每个Agent Skill由一个强制性的SKILL$.$md文件定义，该文件包含元数据和一个非结构化的Markdown正文，其内容完全由技能作者决定。尽管Agent Skills被快速采用，但关于这些文件如何编写以及现有编写指南在实践中是否被遵循，我们知之甚少。在本文中，我们首次对SKILL$.$md文件作为软件工件进行了系统性研究。我们定性分析了238个真实世界技能，并推导出包含13个高层次和44个低层次语义组件的分类法。随后，我们进行了29个来源的多声部文献综述，以确定编写SKILL$.$md文件的最佳实践，并引入了技能异味（skill smells）作为对这些实践的违反。最后，我们开发了一个自动检测器并将其应用于真实世界技能，发现超过99%的SKILL$.$md文件至少包含一个技能异味，且一旦引入，技能异味很少随技能演化而消失。这些发现揭示了推荐实践与实际编写实践之间的显著差距，激励开发自动化技术来修复技能异味，同时提高开发者对这一新兴质量问题的认识。

Original abstract: Agent Skills provide on-demand domain knowledge to LLM agents without requiring model retraining. Each Agent Skill is defined by a mandatory SKILL$.$md file containing metadata and an unstructured Markdown body whose contents are left entirely to the skill author. Despite the rapid adoption of Agent Skills, little is known about how these files are authored or whether existing authoring guidelines are followed in practice. In this paper, we present the first systematic study of SKILL$.$md files as a software artifact. We qualitatively analyze 238 real-world skills and derive a taxonomy of 13 higher-level and 44 lower-level semantic components. We then conduct a multivocal literature review of 29 sources to identify best practices for authoring SKILL$.$md files and introduce skill smells as violations of these practices. Finally, we develop an automated detector and apply it to real-world skills, finding that over 99% of SKILL$.$md files contain at least one skill smell, and once introduced, skill smells rarely disappear as skills evolve. These findings reveal a substantial gap between recommended and actual authoring practices, motivating the development of automated techniques to remediate skill smells while increasing developer awareness of this emerging quality issue.

</details>

*Muhammad Hassan,Carl Gunter,Susan Landau,Masooda Bashir*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 物联网互操作性标准Matter虽有前景，但开发者在实际工作中的体验尚不明确，需要系统性地了解其实现和集成中的问题。

Method: 通过主题建模和定性分析，研究来自官方GitHub仓库的13,000多个问题，识别出四类关注领域。

Result: 识别出测试、互操作性、开发和平台与网络四个主要问题领域，并揭示了这些问题的演变及具体表现。

Conclusion: Matter标准存在系统性的技术和集成挑战，需改进测试基础设施、跨厂商指导和文档以促进其成熟。

中文摘要：Matter旨在解决物联网（IoT）中长期存在的互操作性问题，但关于开发者如何在日常工作中体验该标准，人们知之甚少。本文通过审查来自官方Project CHIP GitHub仓库的超过13,000个问题，来了解贡献者在实施和集成Matter时遇到的问题类型。利用主题建模和定性分析，我们识别出四个反复出现的关注领域：测试、互操作性、开发和平台与网络，并描述了这些问题如何在代码库和工具的演变中显现。研究结果揭示了系统性的技术和集成挑战，并指出了随着标准不断成熟，改进Matter测试基础设施、跨厂商指导和文档的具体机会。

Original abstract: Matter seeks to resolve longstanding interoperability problems in the Internet of Things (IoT), yet little is known about how developers experience the standard in day to day work. This paper examines over 13,000 issues from the official Project CHIP GitHub repository to understand the kinds of problems contributors report when implementing and integrating Matter. Using topic modeling and qualitative analysis, we identify four recurring areas of concern, Testing, Interoperability, Development, and Platform and Network, and describe how they manifest in the evolution of the codebase and tooling. The findings reveal systematic technical and integration challenges and point to concrete opportunities to refine Matter's test infrastructure, cross vendor guidance, and documentation as the standard continues to mature.

</details>


### [44] [Dependencies that Bundle Code and Execution](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02618v1)
*Aman Sharma,Martin Monperrus*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: LIBCACHE是首个通过包注册表分发每个依赖项的执行缓存并合并它们以加速应用启动的系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有系统不将执行状态发布到注册表，导致每次启动需从头重建，效率低下。

Method: 库维护者从其测试套件生成执行缓存并发布到Maven Central，应用构建时合并所有依赖缓存为统一缓存。

Result: 在三个Java项目12个负载上，启动速度提升最高1.91倍，10个负载优于单工作负载缓存，缓存生产增加10-47%构建时间，缓存平均大小为JAR的18倍。

Conclusion: LIBCACHE证明了执行缓存是可分发的供应链工件，合并依赖缓存提供比单次观察更广的启动覆盖。

中文摘要：应用程序由许多依赖项构建而成。每个依赖项由包注册表分发，但只包含编译后的代码，不包含执行状态，因此运行时时每次启动都会从头重建该状态。执行缓存记录此准备结果，以便后续启动可以跳过，但现有系统没有将执行状态发布到注册表供下游消费者重用。我们提出LIBCACHE，第一个通过包注册表将每个依赖项的执行缓存作为一等工件与编译代码一起分发的系统。每个库维护者从库自己的测试套件生成执行缓存，并将其与JAR一起发布到Maven Central。在应用程序构建时，LIBCACHE将所有依赖项的缓存合并为一个统一的缓存，覆盖每个依赖项测试套件中涉及的所有类。我们在三个真实世界的Java项目的12个工作负载上评估LIBCACHE。LIBCACHE将应用程序启动速度提升高达1.91倍，并在12个工作负载中的10个上优于从单个工作负载构建的缓存，batik的平均增益最大（1.60倍对比1.27倍）。缓存生产为应用程序的构建时间增加了10-47%，执行缓存平均大小为对应JAR的18倍。我们的主要贡献是LIBCACHE，它证明了执行缓存是可分发的供应链工件，并且合并每个依赖项的缓存比任何单次观察运行提供更广泛的启动覆盖。

Original abstract: Applications are built from many dependencies. Each dependency is distributed by package registries but it only contains compiled code and does not ship execution state, so runtimes rebuild that state from scratch on every startup. Execution caching records this preparation result so subsequent starts can skip it, but no existing system publishes execution state to a registry for downstream consumers to reuse. We introduce LIBCACHE, the first system to distribute per-dependency execution caches through a package registry as first-class artifacts alongside compiled code. Each library maintainer produces an execution cache from the library's own test suite and publishes it to Maven Central alongside the JAR. At application build time, LIBCACHE merges all per-dependency caches into a single unified cache that covers the classes exercised across every dependency's test suite. We evaluate LIBCACHE on three real-world Java projects across twelve workloads. LIBCACHE speeds up application startup by up to 1.91x and outperforms a cache built from a single workload in 10 of 12 workloads, with the largest average gain for batik (1.60x vs. 1.27x). Cache production adds 10-47% to build time for applications, and execution caches average 18x the size of the corresponding JAR. Our main contribution is LIBCACHE, which establishes that execution caches are distributable supply chain artifacts and that merging per-dependency caches delivers broader startup coverage than any single observation run.

</details>


### [45] [Kani: A Model Checker for Rust](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01504v1)
*Rémi Delmas,Zyad Hassan,Qinheping Hu,Rahul Kumar,Felipe R. Monteiro,Thanh Nguyen,Adrián Palacios,Celina Val,Michael Tautschnig,Justus Adam,Daniel Schwartz-Narbonne,Carolyn Zech*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: Kani是一个Rust模型检查器，通过将MIR编译到CBMC引擎并支持契约语言，实现了对安全属性和功能正确性的自动验证，已在工业项目中发现了多个新bug。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Rust的所有权类型系统虽然防止了内存错误，但不安全操作的正确性、功能正确性和无运行时恐慌等性质仍无法通过编译保证，需要额外的验证手段。

Method: Kani将Rust的MIR证明测试编译到CBMC位精确引擎，自动检查安全属性；并通过提供包含函数契约、循环契约、量词和函数存根的规范语言，将有界验证扩展到无界验证。

Result: 在工业Rust项目的案例研究中，契约功能将验证从无恐慌提升到功能正确性，发现了6个之前未知的bug；在Rust标准库验证活动中，每次代码变更验证超过16,000个测试，展示了大规模应用能力。

Conclusion: Kani是一种可行的、可扩展的Rust模型检查工具，能够在生产环境中提供有界和无界的正确性保证，且已证明其工业实用性。

中文摘要：Rust的所有权类型系统可以防止安全代码中的内存错误，但某些期望的属性仍然独立于编译：不安全操作（例如裸指针解引用）的正确性、功能正确性以及没有运行时恐慌。我们提出了Kani，一个开源的Rust模型检查器，它将有界模型检查从错误发现推进到为这些属性提供正确性保证。Kani将来自Rust中间级表示（MIR）的证明测试编译到CBMC的位精确验证引擎中，自动检查一组全面的安全属性，无需用户注释。为了将验证从有界扩展到无界，Kani提供了一种规范语言，包括函数契约、循环契约、量词和函数存根。我们通过对工业级Rust项目的案例研究证明了可行性，其中契约将验证从无恐慌提升到功能正确性，发现了六个先前未知的错误。Kani在生产环境的持续集成中大规模运行，在Rust标准库验证活动中每次代码变更验证超过16,000个测试。

Original abstract: Rust's ownership type system prevents memory errors in safe code, but certain desirable properties remain orthogonal to compilation: the soundness of unsafe operations (e.g., raw pointer dereferences), functional correctness, and absence of runtime panics. We present Kani, an open-source model checker for Rust that pushes bounded model checking beyond bug-finding to provide correctness guarantees for these properties. Kani compiles proof harnesses from Rust's Mid-level Intermediate Representation (MIR) into CBMC's bit-precise verification engine, automatically checking a comprehensive set of safety properties with no user annotation. To extend verification from bounded to unbounded, Kani provides a specification language comprising function contracts, loop contracts, quantifiers, and function stubbing. We demonstrate feasibility through case studies on industrial Rust projects, where contracts upgraded verification from panic-freedom to functional correctness, uncovering six previously unknown bugs. Kani operates at scale in production CI, with over 16,000 harnesses verified per code change in the Rust standard library verification campaign.

</details>

### [46] [Managed Autonomy at Runtime: Gear-Based Safety and Governance for Single- and Multi-Agent Cyber-Physical Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00334v1)
*Srini Ramaswamy,Wang Miaosheng*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出多agent运行时安全控制框架（档位机制），证明稳定性与安全性，可迁移至coding agent安全控制

TL;DR: 本文提出一种离散时间控制系统，通过执行齿轮和效用门控机制确保自主智能体的安全性和稳定性，并在多智能体场景中实现高异常检测率和低延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主智能体在无持续人类监督时会出现安全违规、行为不稳定和连续性丢失等故障模式，现有方法缺乏形式化保证。

Method: 开发了包含五个执行齿轮（观察、建议、规划、执行、交互）的离散时间控制系统，结合效用门控调度和事件驱动回退；对于多智能体CPS，应用托管自主生命周期，并通过共识门控、Lyapunov分析和会合控制提供分布式保证。

Result: 在三智能体UR5装配单元上，异常检测率达99.6%（基线2.1%），检测延迟降低3.5倍，并提供形式化安全证书。

Conclusion: 执行齿轮作为微级权限，在运行时治理状态下分离动作控制与自主治理，有效提升安全性和稳定性。

中文摘要：自主智能体，无论是LLM驱动的软件智能体还是机器人物理智能体，在缺乏持续人类监督运行时面临一类常见的故障模式：未经验证的行为导致的安全违规、无约束循环导致的行为不稳定，以及未处理错误状态导致的连续性丢失。我们开发了\system{}，一个离散时间控制系统，结合了五个执行齿轮（\Gobs{}、\Gsug{}、\Gplan{}、\Gexec{}、\Gint{}）与效用门控调度和事件驱动的回退。对于单智能体情况，我们证明了单调稳定性、执行安全性、最终稳定、回退完备性，以及与齿轮约束马尔可夫决策过程的等价性。对于多智能体信息物理系统（CPS），我们应用了已建立的\smart{}托管自主生命周期，并将运行时证据映射到其四个治理状态（\Stable{}/\Meta{}/\Assisted{}/\Regulated{}）。共识门控、群体级Lyapunov分析、每个智能体的齿轮权限以及会合控制提供了分布式安全性和稳定性保证，包括在给定假设下的零碰撞。我们在一个三智能体UR5机器人装配单元上评估了生成的运行时，使用来自NIST\emph{机器人手臂位置精度退化测量}数据集的故障幅度，在10,000次蒙特卡洛回合中进行了评估。它实现了99.6％的异常检测率，而单智能体基线为2.1％，检测延迟降低了3.5倍，并提供了正式物理工作空间安全证书。执行齿轮充当\smart{}运行时治理状态下的微级权限，将动作控制与自主治理分离。

Original abstract: Autonomous agents, whether LLM-driven software agents or robotic physical agents, face a common class of failure modes when operating without continuous human oversight: safety violations from unverified actions, behavioral instability from unconstrained loops, and continuity loss from unhandled error states. We develop \system{}, a discrete-time control system that combines five execution gears (\Gobs{}, \Gsug{}, \Gplan{}, \Gexec{}, \Gint{}) with utility-gated dispatch and event-driven fallback. For the single-agent case, we prove monotonic stability, execution safety, eventual stabilization, fallback completeness, and equivalence to a gear-constrained Markov decision process. For multi-agent cyber-physical systems (CPS), we apply the established \smart{} managed-autonomy lifecycle and map runtime evidence into its four governance states (\Stable{}/\Meta{}/\Assisted{}/\Regulated{}). Consensus gating, swarm-level Lyapunov analysis, per-agent gear authority, and rendezvous control provide distributed safety and stability guarantees, including zero collision under the stated assumptions. We evaluate the resulting runtime on a three-agent UR5 robotic assembly cell using fault magnitudes calibrated from the NIST \emph{Degradation Measurement of Robot Arm Position Accuracy} dataset across 10,000 Monte Carlo episodes. It achieves a 99.6\% anomaly detection rate versus 2.1\% for the single-agent baseline, reduces detection latency by $3.5\times$, and supplies a formal physical-workspace safety certificate. The execution gears act as micro-level permissions beneath the \smart{} runtime governance states, separating action control from autonomy governance.

### [47] [Personalization as Inverse Planning: Learning Latent Design Intents for Agentic Slide Generation via Structural Denoising](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00407v1)
*Tianci Liu,Zihan Dong,Linjun Zhang,Haoyu Wang,jing Gao,Emre Kiciman,Ranveer Chandra,Wei-Ting Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出逆规划与多agent强化学习框架用于幻灯片生成，泛化agent规划与协作方法

TL;DR: 提出SPIRE框架，通过结构去噪和多智能体强化学习近似解决页面级幻灯片个性化问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI智能体方法无法捕捉用户深层设计意图，导致页面级幻灯片个性化问题未解决。

Method: 将PSP形式化为逆规划问题，提出SPIRE框架，通过破坏和恢复幻灯片结构，利用两个智能体协同强化学习来优化设计。

Result: 实验表明SPIRE优于现有方法，且结构去噪是PSP的一致替代目标，多智能体降低策略梯度方差。

Conclusion: SPIRE有效解决了页面级幻灯片个性化问题，无需工具知识即可学习设计意图。

中文摘要：幻灯片设计需要个性化定制演示文稿主题和页面布局。然而，当前基于AI智能体的方法难以处理细粒度的页面级设计。它们仅依赖于预定义模板或用户冗长指令，无法捕捉潜在的设计意图，导致页面级幻灯片个性化（PSP）问题未能解决。为弥补这一差距，本工作将PSP形式化为逆规划问题。我们提出学习设计意图，而不假设使用任何特定执行工具（如PowerPoint、Beamer）的知识。然而，放弃对这些工具的控制使得端到端优化问题变得棘手。为此，我们提出SPIRE，一个近似求解PSP的原则性框架。通过有意破坏干净幻灯片的视觉结构，SPIRE创建了一个可验证的去噪任务，其中两个智能体通过强化学习（RL）协作学习优化可执行设计。我们证明了结构去噪是PSP的一致替代目标，并且多智能体公式严格降低了RL中的策略梯度方差。大量实验证明了SPIRE的优越性。

Original abstract: Slide design requires personalizing both deck themes and page layouts. Yet, current AI agent-based methods struggle with fine-grained, page-level design. Solely relying on prespecified templates or user verbose instructions, they fail to capture latent design intents, leaving Page-level Slide Personalization (PSP) unresolved. To close this gap, this work formulates PSP as an inverse planning problem. We propose to learn a design intent without assuming any knowledge of the specific executing tools (e.g., PowerPoint, Beamer) being used. However, relinquishing control over these tools makes the problem intractable to optimize end-to-end. To overcome this, we propose SPIRE, a principled framework to solve PSP approximately. By intentionally corrupting the visual structures of clean slides, SPIRE creates a verifiable task to denoise the corruption, whereby two agents learn to collaboratively refine executable designs via reinforcement learning (RL). We present a proof that structural denoising is a consistent surrogate for PSP, and that the multi-agent formulation strictly reduces policy gradient variance in RL. Extensive experiments demonstrate the superiority of SPIRE.

### [48] [PHREEQC-MCQ-200: A Diagnostic Benchmark for Tool-Augmented Scientific Simulator Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00436v1)
*Ke Zhang,Sahchit Chundur,Mohammad Javad Qomi,Maziar Raissi*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 工具增强的科学模拟器Agent基准，其轨迹验证和输出接口设计对编码Agent评测有启发。

TL;DR: 提出了PHREEQC-MCQ-200基准，评估工具增强型代理在水地球化学模拟中的可靠性，发现工具使用虽提高平均准确性但存在非单调退化，输出协议影响性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估忽视工具使用中的退化现象，需要端到端诊断框架。

Method: 构建包含200道多项选择题的基准，要求代理执行完整模拟流程，分析不同模型和输出协议下的表现。

Result: 工具访问提高平均准确性但存在非单调退化；目录界面节省成本但影响中端模型；项目级保留和输出敏感性重要。

Conclusion: 科学代理评估应报告多项指标，如项目级保留和输出访问敏感性。

中文摘要：大型语言模型代理越来越多地连接到科学软件，但尚不清楚工具访问何时使科学计算更可靠而非仅仅更复杂。我们引入了PHREEQC-MCQ-200，一个用于评估工具增强型代理在确定性水地球化学模拟上的基准。该基准包含200道多项选择题，源自21个经过验证的PHREEQC场景，要求代理构建模拟器输入、执行PHREEQC、检查结构化输出并提交最终答案。在多个前沿和中端模型系列中，模拟器访问显著提高了总体准确性，确认了对于许多科学计算任务，基于实地的执行是必要的。然而，增益并非单调：工具增强型代理也会丢失它们在没有工具时正确回答的项目，揭示了仅平均准确性隐藏的退化。我们进一步展示了输出访问协议的重要性。目录界面可以减少令牌成本，同时保持或提高较强模型的准确性，但会降低无法可靠导航结构化模拟器输出的中端模型的性能。因此，PHREEQC-MCQ-200将科学工具使用视为端到端的诊断问题，而非简单的工具调用能力。我们认为，科学代理的评估不仅应报告准确性，还应报告项目级保留、输出访问敏感性、轨迹失败以及计算链断裂的位置。

Original abstract: Large language model agents are increasingly connected to scientific software, yet it remains unclear when tool access makes scientific computation more reliable rather than merely more complex. We introduce PHREEQC-MCQ-200, a benchmark for evaluating tool-augmented agents on deterministic aqueous-geochemistry simulations. The benchmark contains 200 multiple-choice questions derived from 21 validated PHREEQC scenarios, requiring agents to construct simulator inputs, execute PHREEQC, inspect structured outputs, and commit to final answers.
  Across multiple frontier and mid-tier model families, simulator access substantially improves aggregate accuracy, confirming that grounded execution is necessary for many scientific-computation tasks. However, the gains are not monotonic: tool-augmented agents also lose items they answered correctly without tools, revealing regressions that average accuracy alone hides. We further show that output-access protocol matters. A table-of-contents interface can reduce token cost while preserving or improving accuracy for stronger models, but it degrades performance for mid-tier models that cannot reliably navigate structured simulator outputs.
  PHREEQC-MCQ-200 therefore frames scientific tool use as an end-to-end diagnostic problem rather than a simple tool-calling capability. We argue that evaluations of scientific agents should report not only accuracy, but also item-level retention, output-access sensitivity, trajectory failures, and where the computation chain breaks.

### [49] [Agri-SAGE: Simulation-Grounded Multi-Agent LLM for Context-Aware Agricultural Advisory Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00454v1)
*Vedant Balasubramaniam,Geetha Charan,Manojkumar Patil,Rohit P Suresh,V Priyanka,Kodur Sai Vinay Sathvik,Y. Narahari*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了Agri-SAGE框架，集成检索增强的多智能体LLM推理和APSIM生物物理模拟，评估了Plan-and-Solve、思维树和Reflexion三种推理方法。

Result: 三种方法均显著优于静态PoP基线，思维树实现最高峰值产量，Reflexion以较低计算成本达到可比农艺效果。

中文摘要：农业咨询系统面临一个基本矛盾：静态的农艺指南提供一致、基于证据的建议，但对季节内变异和动态不确定性视而不见。最近由大语言模型驱动的咨询系统容易产生另一种风险：生成农艺上可信但生理上不令人信服的建议。Agri-SAGE是一个闭环框架，通过将基于检索的多智能体大语言模型推理与基于APSIM的生物物理模拟相结合，旨在解决上述两个局限性，以生成和验证农艺咨询。为了评估这一框架，我们评估了三种推理方法，即Plan-and-Solve、思维树和Reflexion，进行了为期10年的回顾性分析。这三种方法均显著优于静态PoP（实践包）基线，其中思维树实现了令人印象深刻的峰值产量。同时，Reflexion通过利用跨季节情景记忆，以显著更低的计算成本实现了可比的农艺效果。

Original abstract: Agricultural advisory systems face a fundamental tension: static agronomic guidelines offer consistent, evidence-based recommendations, yet remain blind to in-season variability and dynamic uncertainties. Recent advisory systems powered by LLMs are liable for a different risk of generating recommendations that are agronomically credible but physiologically unconvincing. Agri-SAGE is a closed-loop framework designed to resolve the above two limitations by integrating retrieval-grounded multi-agent LLM reasoning with APSIM-based biophysical simulation, to generate and validate agronomic advisories. To assess this framework, we evaluate three reasoning approaches, namely Plan-and-Solve, Tree of Thoughts, and Reflexion, over a 10-year retrospective analysis. All three significantly outperform static PoP (Package-of-Practice) baselines, with Tree of Thoughts achieving impressive peak yields. At the same time, Reflexion achieves comparable agronomic outcomes at substantially lower computational cost by leveraging cross-seasonal episodic memory.

### [50] [Multi-scale Mixture of World Models for Embodied Agents in Evolving Environments](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00457v1)
*Jinwoo Jang,Daniel J. Rho,Sihyung Yoon,Hyunsuk Cho,Honguk Woo*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 具身Agent多尺度世界模型混合架构，其路由与自适应更新方法可迁移至通用Agent设计。

TL;DR: MuSix通过两阶段路由和尺度相关遗忘率实现了具身代理的多尺度知识混合与动态适应，在EmbodiedBench和HAZARD上超越基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有混合专家（MoE）应用于具身代理时缺乏显式尺度路由和统一更新策略，无法适应多尺度知识的差异化过时速率。

Method: 提出MuSix框架，包含两阶段路由：元路由将经验距离映射到连续尺度空间权重，基础路由选择具体世界模型；以及尺度依赖的遗忘率和门控跨尺度转移实现分层适应。

Result: 在EmbodiedBench和HAZARD基准上，MuSix在多尺度推理和动态适应任务中优于所有基线方法。

Conclusion: MuSix通过尺度感知的路由和演化有效解决了具身代理中多尺度知识混合与适应问题，提升了动态环境下的性能。

中文摘要：在现实世界中运行的具身代理需要随着条件变化进行多尺度推理和知识适应。我们发现将混合专家（MoE）应用于此场景时存在两个挑战：路由缺乏明确的尺度概念，无法在特定尺度上进行目标更新；且统一更新策略无法适应每个尺度知识过时的不同速率。我们提出了MuSix，一个通过尺度感知的世界模型混合与演化来解决这两个挑战的框架。两阶段路由机制将尺度选择基于经验距离——一种受解释水平理论启发的情境新颖性度量：元路由首先将该量映射到连续尺度空间上的权重，然后每个尺度的基础路由在识别出的尺度内选择世界模型。对于适应，尺度相关的遗忘率允许低尺度知识快速更新，而高尺度抽象持久存在，并且门控跨尺度转移保持了层次结构中的一致性。在EmbodiedBench和HAZARD上的实验表明，MuSix在多尺度推理和动态适应方面优于最先进的基线方法。

Original abstract: Embodied agents operating in the real world require multi-scale reasoning and knowledge adaptation as conditions change. We identify two challenges in applying Mixture of Experts (MoE) to this setting: routing lacks an explicit notion of scale, preventing targeted updates at specific scales, and a uniform update policy cannot accommodate the different rates at which knowledge at each scale becomes outdated. We present MuSix, a framework that addresses both challenges through scale-aware world model mixture and evolution. A two-stage routing mechanism grounds scale selection in experiential distance, a measure of situational novelty inspired by Construal Level Theory: a meta-router first maps this quantity to a weight over continuous scale space, then per-scale base routers select world models within the identified scale. For adaptation, scale-dependent forgetting rates allow low-scale knowledge to refresh rapidly while high-scale abstractions persist, and gated inter-scale transfer maintains coherence across the hierarchy. Experiments on EmbodiedBench and HAZARD show that MuSix improves over state-of-the-art baselines on multi-scale reasoning and dynamic adaptation.

### [51] [AGI Maze as a Benchmark Framework for World-Modeling Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00627v1)
*Alexey Potapov*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出AGI Maze基准框架，评估LLM agent在部分可观测环境中的世界建模能力，属于通用agent评测，可迁移至coding agent环境理解

TL;DR: AGI Maze 框架测试了LLM在需要记忆和世界状态表示的迷宫任务中的表现，发现普通LLM无法在推理时内部表示迷宫，即使使用消息历史作为工作记忆也难以可靠解决小迷宫。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM在处理部分可观测、有状态且需要记忆和隐藏状态假设的任务时表现不佳，因此需要创建基准测试来衡量其学习并使用世界状态表示的能力。

Method: 设计AGI Maze框架，提供基于网格的迷宫任务和多个难度级别；初步评估普通LLM在简单迷宫上的表现，并引入一个允许使用消息历史作为工作记忆的基线智能体。

Result: 普通LLM在推理时无法内部表示迷宫；基线智能体（使用消息历史）性能有所提升，但在远超人类所需步数的预算内仍无法可靠解决小迷宫。

Conclusion: 当前LLM在需要持久世界状态表示和结构化假设的推理任务上表现不足，AGI Maze框架为衡量此类能力提供了有用的基准。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）是强大的模式补全系统，但其默认操作模式——从静态上下文中预测下一个词元——并不能可靠地产生持久的、可操作的外部世界表示。许多在文本中看起来像“推理”的任务一旦环境部分可观测、有状态且需要对隐藏状态进行记忆和结构化假设时，就会变得困难得多。AGI Maze是一个轻量级框架，用于构建此类环境，无需高维感官输入。它提供了一系列基于网格的迷宫任务，具有简洁的API和多个难度级别。目标是创建基准测试，其中智能体必须学习并使用世界状态表示，而不仅仅是从现成的观测中推断局部规则。我们初步评估了几个普通LLM在简单迷宫上的表现，表明它们在LLM推理时无法内部表示迷宫。我们还引入了一个基线智能体，该智能体被允许使用其消息历史作为工作记忆，在智能体运行时构建观测描述。尽管这可以提高性能，但对于LLM智能体来说，即使在小迷宫上，在远超人类所需步数的预算内仍然无法可靠地解决。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are powerful pattern-completion systems, but their default operating mode - predicting the next token from a static context - does not reliably produce persistent, manipulable representations of an external world. Many tasks that look like "reasoning" in text become substantially harder once the environment is partially observable, stateful, and requires memory and structured hypotheses about hidden state. AGI Maze is a lightweight framework for building such environments without requiring high-dimensional sensory inputs. It provides a family of grid-based maze tasks with a clean API and multiple difficulty regimes. The goal is to create benchmarks where agents must learn and use world state representations, not just infer a local rule over readily provided observations. We provide an initial evaluation of several vanilla LLMs on simple mazes showing that they fail to represent mazes internally at LLM inference time. We also introduce a baseline agent, which is allowed to use its message history as a working memory to construct descriptions of observations at agentic runtime. Although this can improve performance, it is still insufficient for an LLM agent to reliably solve even small mazes within a step budget that is more than enough for humans.

### [52] [Coachable agents for interactive gameplay](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00642v1)
*Roberto Capobianco,Harm van Seijen,Nolan D. Bard,Neil Burch,Fatima Davelouis,Josh Davidson,Alisa Devlic,Yunshu Du,Ishan Durugkar,Siddhant Gangapurwala,Daniel Hernandez,G. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有强化学习通常只学习单一最优策略，但许多实际场景需要用户实时控制任务解决方式（风格）。

Method: 将通用价值函数逼近器（UVFA）与精心选择的训练场景、学习算法和数据增强相结合，构建能够学习多种风格的框架。

Result: 在《地平线：西之绝境》、《Gran Turismo》和人形行走三个不同领域中，智能体均能保持对风格请求的一致性，同时完成主要任务。

Conclusion: 该技术使最终用户可以在运行时灵活选择行为，从而对智能体的执行性能进行实时控制。

中文摘要：强化学习已被证明是创建先进人工智能和机器人系统的宝贵工具，为从游戏到机器人再到基础模型的各种领域做出了贡献。通过试错，这些AI系统通常学习一种近乎最优的行为来解决其任务。然而，在许多用例中，人们希望能够对任务的解决方式施加一定程度的控制，最好是实时的。我们将这些对核心任务的修改称为风格。我们将通用价值函数逼近器（UVFAs）与精心选择的训练场景、学习算法和数据增强相结合，创建了一个框架，用于训练在复杂领域中表现出风格的智能体。我们展示了该框架在AAA级视频游戏《地平线：西之绝境》和《Gran Turismo》中的应用，以及在一个开源的人形测试领域中的应用。尽管这些领域性质不同——赛车、风格化的游戏战斗和人形行走——每个智能体都表现出对风格请求的强烈一致性，同时仍然满足其领域中的主要任务。重要的是，本文概述的技术允许最终用户在运行时选择最终行为，从而为他们提供了对最终执行性能的灵活控制。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning has proven to be a valuable tool in the creation of advanced AI and robotic systems, contributing to everything from game playing to robotics to foundation models. Through trial-and-error, these AI systems typically learn one, near-optimal behavior to solve their tasks. However, there are many use cases in which one would like to assert some level of control, preferably in real time, over how the task is solved. We refer to these modifications of a core task as styles. We combine universal value function approximators (UVFAs) with carefully selected training scenarios, learning algorithms, and data augmentation to create a framework for coaching agents that exhibit styles in complex domains. We demonstrate the framework's application in the AAA video games Horizon Forbidden West and Gran Turismo, and in an open-source humanoid test domain. Despite the different nature of the domains -- car racing, stylized game combat, and humanoid walking -- each agent shows strong coherence to the style requests while still satisfying the main task in its domain. Importantly, the techniques outlined in this paper allow an end user to choose the final behavior at run time, giving them flexible control over the final executed performance.

</details>


### [53] [Self-GC: Self-Governing Context for Long-Horizon LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00692v1)
*Xubin Hao,Hongjin Meng,Xin Yin,Jiawei Zhu,Chenpeng Cao*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出Self-GC长程LLM agent上下文管理框架，通过索引化对象和侧信道规划实现高效生命周期控制，直接应用于coding agent长程执行

TL;DR: Self-GC通过将代理上下文对象化并利用侧通道计划器进行折叠、屏蔽和剪枝，实现了高效的长程上下文管理，显著减少令牌使用且不影响未来延续。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有长程LLM代理的上下文管理依赖启发式或最终总结，前者忽略未来依赖，后者丢失精确信息，需要更精细的生命周期控制。

Method: 将用户轮次、工具范围和技能状态转为索引对象，由侧通道计划器提议折叠、屏蔽和剪枝操作，执行器实施可恢复边车、安全提交和缓存感知提交。

Result: 在Hard Set上剪枝43.95%前缀令牌，84.85%未来延续不受影响；在332会话套件上无影响率达91.27%-94.58%，基线最高87.46%；生产中日均输入令牌减少10%-15%，峰值接近20%。

Conclusion: 上下文管理应作为运行时对索引化、可恢复对象的生命周期控制，而非事后文本清理。

中文摘要：长程LLM代理会积累工具结果、文件、计划以及用户约束，这些内容结构过于复杂，无法被视为可丢弃的文本后缀。当前系统主要依赖于运行时的启发式方法（如按时间顺序剪枝和工具输出屏蔽）或接近上下文限制时的最终自我总结。启发式方法成本低，但对未来依赖关系视而不见；总结虽然保留了叙述状态，但往往隐藏了确切的证据、定位器和可编辑的工件。我们提出了Self-GC，其中GC代表自管理上下文，同时有意呼应垃圾回收：系统不仅回收未使用的令牌，而且管理代理上下文对象的生命周期。Self-GC将用户轮次、工具范围和技能状态转变为索引对象；要求侧通道计划器提出折叠、屏蔽和剪枝操作；并让执行器强制实施可恢复的边车、安全的提交边界和缓存感知的提交。在33个会话的Hard Set上，Self-GC剪枝了43.95%的前缀令牌，同时使84.85%的未来延续不受影响，而启发式基线的无影响率为54.55%到69.70%。在332个会话的生产衍生套件上，三个计划器骨干网络的无影响率达到91.27%到94.58%，而基线保持在77.71%到87.46%。在生产中，在线账户级别分割使日间平均输入令牌减少10%到15%，峰值减少接近20%。这些结果表明，上下文管理是运行时对索引化、可恢复对象的生命周期控制，而非事后文本清理。

Original abstract: Long-horizon LLM agents accumulate tool results, files, plans, and user constraints that are too structured to be treated as a disposable text suffix. Current systems mostly rely on in-run heuristics such as chronological pruning and tool-output masking, or on final self-summary near a context limit. Heuristics are cheap but blind to future dependencies; summaries preserve narrative state but often hide exact evidence, locators, and editable artifacts. We present Self-GC, where GC denotes self-governing context while deliberately echoing garbage collection: the system does not merely reclaim unused tokens, but governs the lifecycle of agent context objects. Self-GC turns user turns, tool spans, and skill state into indexed objects; asks a side-channel planner to propose fold, mask, and prune actions; and lets the harness enforce recoverable sidecars, safe commit boundaries, and cache-aware commit. On a 33-session Hard Set, Self-GC prunes 43.95% of prefix tokens while leaving 84.85% of future continuations unaffected, compared with no-impact rates of 54.55% to 69.70% for heuristic baselines. On a 332-session production-derived suite, three planner backbones reach no-impact rates of 91.27% to 94.58%, while baselines remain at 77.71% to 87.46%. In production, an online account-level split reduces daytime average input tokens by 10% to 15%, with peak reductions near 20%. These results point to context management as runtime lifecycle control over indexed, recoverable objects rather than post hoc text cleanup.

</details>


### [54] [Self-Evolving Agents with Anytime-Valid Certificates](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00871v1)
*Biswa Sengupta*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 自进化Agent框架，可审计证书与验证循环，直接适用自动代码优化Agent的安全控制

TL;DR: 提出了SEA架构，通过冻结基础模型和随时有效的门控机制实现安全可控的自进化，在SWE-bench上验证了其对强基础模型的提升效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自进化智能体违反了大多数学习理论保证的假设，需要一种能安全限制自我修改并保持可审计性的架构。

Method: SEA架构：冻结基础模型，使用转向适配器和版本化封装，通过随时有效的门控机制（基于固定错误预算）接受修改；结合五个循环控制器和五个验证器在环机制（最佳N选、微步搜索、自创生复制预言、搜索层控制、自我修复）提供密集信号。

Result: 在SWE-bench验证子集的52个实例上，基础能力是主导效应；在强基础模型（GLM 5.2和GPT）上，隔离贡献分别提升4和5个百分点（GPT从29到34，即65%最佳），事件日志确认机制有效且无回归。

Conclusion: SEA架构有效提升了强基础模型的性能，但结果为单次运行，未来需评估运行间方差并自适应调整算法组合。

中文摘要：自进化智能体违反了大多数学习理论保证背后的假设：数据、评估器、组件和假设空间都是由正在更新的策略产生的。我们提出了SEA，一种架构，它将自我修改限制在一个小的转向适配器和一个围绕冻结基础模型的版本化封装上，并且仅通过一个随时有效的门控机制接受每次修改，该门控机制针对固定的错误预算发出可审计的证书。五个循环控制器组合了已发布的保证；由于这样的门控只能选择冻结基础已经产生的行为，五个验证器在环机制——最佳N选、微步搜索、自创生复制预言、搜索层控制和自我修复——提供了门控所需的密集的无评分信号，仅从问题文本计算得出。在52个实例的SWE-bench验证子集上，跨越四个基础模型，基础能力是主导的、无混杂的效应，并且在两个强基础模型上，一个故意无操作复合控制隔离了该套件的贡献，分别为+4和+5（GLM 5.2从24到28；GPT从29到34，最佳65%），事件日志确认其机制触发并防止了回归。结果是单次运行的昂贵评估；确认运行间方差和调整每任务算法组合是未来工作。

Original abstract: Self-evolving agents violate the assumption behind most learning-theoretic guarantees: the data, evaluator, components, and hypothesis space are produced by the policy being updated. We present \textbf{SEA}, an architecture that confines self-modification to a small steering adapter and a versioned harness around a \emph{frozen} base model and admits each modification only through an anytime-valid gate that emits an auditable certificate against a fixed error budget. Five loop controllers compose published guarantees; because such gates can only \emph{select} among behaviors the frozen base already produces, five verifier-in-the-loop mechanisms -- best-of-$N$, micro-step search, self-authored reproduction oracles, search-layer control, and self-repair -- supply the dense, grader-free signal the gates require, computed from the issue text alone. On a $52$-instance SWE-bench Verified subset across four base models, base capability is the dominant, confound-free effect, and on two strong base models a deliberate no-op-composite control isolates the suite's contribution at $+4$ and $+5$ (\textsc{Glm}~5.2 $24\to28$; \textsc{Gpt} $29\to34$, the $65\%$ best), with event logs confirming that its mechanisms fire and prevent regressions. Results are single-run on expensive evaluations; confirming run-to-run variance and adapting the per-task algorithm mix are future work.

</details>


### [55] [In-Context Reinforcement Learning under Non-Stationarity: A Survey](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11906v1)
*A Run,Ziluo Ding*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 非平稳环境下上下文强化学习综述，对Agent在线适应方法有系统总结，可迁移至Coding Agent

TL;DR: 本文综述了非平稳环境下的上下文强化学习（ICRL），探讨了当任务动态变化时，代理如何仅通过固定参数的策略利用上下文信息进行适应，并按照变化类型、变化方式和可观察性三个维度组织文献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有ICRL研究主要关注平稳设置，忽视了环境非平稳性带来的独特挑战——累积上下文可能过时或误导，需要代理动态判断哪些历史信息仍然有效。

Method: 采用综述方法，定义非平稳ICRL问题，将其与元强化学习、决策序列建模、检索增强RL等关联，并按照“什么变化”、“变化如何发生”和“变化对代理的可观察性”三个问题组织分类。

Result: 系统梳理了非平稳ICRL的相关工作，指出了现有研究在变化类型、变化规律和可观测性方面的分类框架，并揭示了该领域尚未充分探索的方向。

Conclusion: 非平稳ICRL是一个值得关注的研究方向，需要更深入的理论和算法设计，以处理环境变化带来的挑战，并提出了未来可能的研究路径。

中文摘要：决策预训练变换器、算法蒸馏、长上下文元强化学习和检索增强代理的发展重新引起了人们对上下文强化学习（ICRL）的兴趣：预训练或微调的决策模型能够从交互上下文中推断潜在任务规则并改进未来行为，而无需在测试时更新参数。这一研究方向探讨了试验-错误证据、奖励、转移、演示、反馈或检索到的经验如何在上下文窗口内实现类似学习的计算。然而，现有的ICRL综述主要围绕预训练目标、架构、上下文格式、评估协议和理论机制来组织领域，而非平稳设置尚未得到充分研究。在不断变化的环境中，累积的上下文不仅仅是关于固定任务的更多证据：奖励规范、转移核、观察通道、动作接口、约束模型或演示和记忆分布可能偏离当前体制。以前有用的上下文可能变得陈旧、误导，或者在旧体制回归时再次变得有用。我们将非平稳ICRL定义为在部署策略参数保持不变的情况下，通过上下文进行适应的问题：策略必须推断当前决策规则以及累积证据中哪些部分仍然支持该规则。我们定义了非平稳ICRL，并将其与元强化学习、决策序列建模、检索增强强化学习、值和模型感知ICRL以及奖励反馈代理相关联，并沿着三个问题组织文献：什么变化、变化如何发生以及变化对代理的可观察性如何。

Original abstract: The development of decision-pretrained transformers, algorithm distillation, long-context meta-RL, and retrieval-augmented agents has renewed interest in in-context reinforcement learning (ICRL): the ability of a pretrained or fine-tuned decision model to infer latent task rules and improve future behavior from interaction context, without test-time parameter updates. This line of work asks when trial-and-error evidence, rewards, transitions, demonstrations, feedback, or retrieved experience can make learning-like computation happen inside the context window. However, existing surveys of ICRL mainly organize the field around pretraining objectives, architectures, context formats, evaluation protocols, and theoretical mechanisms, while the non-stationary setting remains comparatively underexamined. In changing environments, accumulated context is not merely more evidence about a fixed task: the reward specification, transition kernel, observation channel, action interface, constraint model, or demonstration and memory distribution can fall out of alignment with the current regime. Previously useful context can therefore become stale, misleading, or useful again when an old regime returns. We survey non-stationary ICRL as the problem of adapting through context while deployed policy parameters remain fixed: the policy must infer both the current decision rule and which parts of its accumulated evidence still support that rule. We define non-stationary ICRL, relate it to meta-RL, decision sequence modeling, retrieval-augmented RL, value- and model-aware ICRL, and reward-feedback agents, and organize the literature along three questions: what changes, how the change unfolds, and how observable the change is to the agent.

### [56] [Bayesian Uncertainty Propagation for Agentic RAG Pipelines: A Proof-of-Concept Study on Multi-Hop Question Answering](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00972v1)
*Louis Donaldson,Connor Walker,Koorosh Aslansefat,Yiannis Papadopoulos*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: Agentic RAG中贝叶斯不确定性传播框架，含规划、评估、生成多阶段，可迁移至coding agent可靠性评估。

TL;DR: 提出一种基于贝叶斯网络传播不确定性信号的智能RAG框架，在HotpotQA上表现更优，但在StrategyQA上因校准问题受限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为确保Agentic RAG系统的可信赖部署，需要估计多阶段推理流程的失败可能性，当前缺乏有效的系统级不确定性监测机制。

Method: 构建不确定性感知的Agentic RAG框架，从规划器、评估器和生成器阶段提取基于语义分歧和自评估的不确定性信号，并通过贝叶斯网络传播以计算系统级和节点级不确定性。

Result: 在HotpotQA上，贝叶斯传播有效累积多跳推理的不确定性，AUROC等指标优于基线；在StrategyQA上，由于上游信号误校准和不可靠，性能受限。

Conclusion: 贝叶斯不确定性传播是监测Agentic RAG系统的有前景但初步的机制，需在海上风电等工业领域进一步验证。

中文摘要：可信赖地部署智能检索增强生成（Agentic RAG）系统需要机制来估计多阶段推理流程何时可能失败。本文提出了一种不确定性感知的智能检索增强生成（RAG）框架，其中规划器、评估器和生成器阶段产生源自语义分歧和生成器自评估的不确定性信号。这些信号通过贝叶斯网络（BN）传播，以估计系统级不确定性，并提供跨工作流程潜在故障点的节点级指标。该方法在StrategyQA和HotpotQA上使用GPT-3.5-Turbo和GPT-4.1-Nano进行评估，采用受试者工作特征曲线下面积（AUROC）、准确率-拒绝曲线下面积（AUARC）、期望校准误差（ECE）和Brier分数来评估判别能力、选择性预测和校准。结果表明，贝叶斯传播在HotpotQA上更有效，其中不确定性在多跳推理阶段累积，而StrategyQA则暴露了由于误校准和不可靠上游信号导致的局限性。该研究将贝叶斯不确定性传播定位为一种有前景但初步的监测智能RAG系统机制，需要在工业领域（如海上风电（OSW）维护决策支持）中进行未来验证。

Original abstract: Trustworthy deployment of Agentic Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) systems requires mechanisms for estimating when multi-stage reasoning pipelines may fail. This paper presents an uncertainty-aware Agentic Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) framework in which planner, evaluator and generator stages produce uncertainty signals derived from semantic divergence and generator self-evaluation. These signals are propagated through a Bayesian Network (BN) to estimate system-level uncertainty and provide node-level indicators of potential failure points across the workflow. The approach is evaluated on StrategyQA and HotpotQA using GPT-3.5-Turbo and GPT-4.1-Nano, with Area Under the Receiver Operating Characteristic Curve (AUROC), Area Under the Accuracy-Rejection Curve (AUARC), Expected Calibration Error (ECE), and Brier Score used to assess discrimination, selective prediction and calibration. Results show that Bayesian propagation is more effective on HotpotQA, where uncertainty accumulates across multi-hop reasoning stages, while StrategyQA exposes limitations caused by miscalibration and unreliable upstream signals. The study positions Bayesian uncertainty propagation as a promising but preliminary mechanism for monitoring Agentic RAG systems, with future validation required in industrial domains such as Offshore Wind (OSW) maintenance decision support.

### [57] [Agentic generation of verifiable rules for deterministic, self-expanding reaction classification](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01061v3)
*Daniel Armstrong,Maarten Dobbelaere,Valentas Olikauskas,Helena Avila,Octavian Susanu,Jérôme Waser,Philippe Schwaller*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent LLM框架自主生成并验证化学反应规则，含验证循环和自动扩展，可迁移至代码优化规则生成。

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于多智能体LLM的自动化流水线，能从专利数据中自动生成反应规则，将分类从68类扩展到14,073类，分类准确率达97.7%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有计算机辅助合成规划依赖固定规则集，无法适应新化学反应，且手动编码不可行。

Method: 构建多智能体LLM框架，自动从US专利反应中分类并编写反应规则，通过验证循环测试规则。

Result: 分类从68类扩展到14,073类，未见过反应分类准确率97.7%，与领先专有分类器相当。

Conclusion: 该方法生成了活的反应性数据库，提供了将生成模型转化为可靠、自扩展符号系统的通用途径。

中文摘要：计算机辅助合成规划通过使用大型反应规则库将目标分子分解为可获得的 precursors，每个规则为每个转化赋予一个确定性的、可解释的标签。但化学是长尾分布的，使得手动编码难以处理，现有工具依赖于无法适应新化学反应的固定规则集。本文提出了一个全自动流水线，其中由大型语言模型（LLMs）组成的多智能体框架对反应进行分类并自行编写规则，涉及665,901项美国专利反应，每个规则在验证循环中生成，并在语料库中进行测试。它将标准分类从68类扩展到14,073类，无需人工筛选。通过轻量级指纹分类器，它对未见过反应的分类准确率达到97.7%，与领先的专有分类器相当，同时更精细地解析化学，并可按需扩展到其训练分布之外的化学领域。结果是一个活的反应性数据库，以及将生成模型转化为可靠、可自扩展符号系统的通用途径。

Original abstract: Computer-assisted synthesis planning breaks target molecules into accessible precursors using large libraries of reaction rules that assign each transformation a deterministic, interpretable label. But chemistry is long-tailed, making manual encoding intractable, and existing tools rely on fixed rulesets that cannot adapt to new chemistries. Here we present a fully automated pipeline in which a multi-agent framework of large language models (LLMs) classifies reactions and writes the rules themselves across 665,901 US patent reactions, generating each rule under a verification loop that tests it against the corpus. It expands a standard taxonomy from 68 to 14,073 classes without human curation. With a lightweight fingerprint classifier, it classifies 97.7\% of unseen reactions, matching a leading proprietary classifier while resolving chemistry more finely and extending on demand to chemistry outside its training distribution. The result is a living reactivity database and a general route to turning generative models into reliable, self-expanding symbolic systems.

### [58] [Can Agents Generalize to the Open World? Unveiling the Fragility of Static Training in Tool Use](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01084v1)
*Song-Lin Lv,Weiming Wu,Rui Zhu,Zi-Jian Cheng,Lan-Zhe Guo*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 直接研究LLM Agent在开放世界中的泛化与工具使用脆弱性，核心相关。

TL;DR: 形式化OpenAgent问题设置，构建沙盒环境分析LLM代理在开放环境中的性能退化，并提出扰动增强微调策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM代理在静态基准中表现良好，但难以适应现实世界中动态变化的用户查询、工具集和交互动态，存在泛化差距。

Method: 形式化OpenAgent问题设置，构建多层级的沙盒环境，提出扰动增强微调（Perturbation-Augmented Fine-Tuning）作为SFT的干预策略。

Result: 通过实验发现，无论是SFT还是强化学习训练的代理，在开放环境变化下均出现不同程度的性能下降。

Conclusion: 扰动增强微调有助于提升代理在现实环境中的鲁棒性和实用性，为后续研究奠定基础。

中文摘要：虽然大型语言模型（LLM）代理在静态基准测试中表现出色，但它们在现实场景中的部署受到用户查询、工具集和交互动态的动态性质的阻碍。为了解决这一泛化差距，我们形式化了OpenAgent（开放世界中的工具使用代理），这是一个以查询、动作、观察和领域维度上的分布变化为特征的问题设置。为了系统地诊断其影响，我们构建了一个受控的沙盒环境，在其中我们定义了跨四个层级的细粒度环境变化：感知、交互、推理和内化，并进行了一系列全面的实验。我们的分析得出一系列关键见解，表明通过监督微调（SFT）和强化学习训练的代理在面对开放环境变化时都会遭受不同程度的性能下降。基于这些见解，我们提出了扰动增强微调，这是一种基于干扰的SFT干预策略，为增强代理在现实环境中的鲁棒性和实用性奠定了基础。我们的代码将在以下地址发布：https://github.com/LAMDA-NeSy/OpenAgent。

Original abstract: While Large Language Model (LLM) agents demonstrate proficiency in static benchmarks, their deployment in real-world scenarios is hindered by the dynamic nature of user queries, tool sets, and interaction dynamics. To address this generalization gap, we formalize OpenAgent (Tool-Use Agent in Open-World), a problem setting characterized by distributional shifts across query, action, observation, and domain dimensions. To systematically diagnose its impact, we construct a controlled sandbox environment where we define fine-grained environmental shifts across a four-tier hierarchy, Perception, Interaction, Reasoning, and Internalization, and conduct a comprehensive series of experiments. Our analysis yields a series of key insights, demonstrating that agents trained via both Supervised Fine-Tuning(SFT) and Reinforcement Learning suffer from varying degrees of performance degradation when confronting open environmental shifts. Building on these insights, we propose Perturbation-Augmented Fine-Tuning, a disturbance-based intervention strategy for SFT that lays the foundation for enhancing agent robustness and utility in realistic environments. Our code will be released at: https://github. com/LAMDA-NeSy/OpenAgent.

### [59] [Theoria: Rewrite-Acceptability Verification over Informal Reasoning States](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01223v3)
*Michael Saldivar,Ben Slivinski*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出Theoria验证架构，通过类型化状态转换和可审计理由实现AI答案的可信认证，在专家问题上达到91.4%精确度，并有效检测隐藏前提和捏造引用等错误。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法中，形式化证明辅助工具确定但覆盖有限，LLM评判器覆盖广但分数不透明且难以审计，需要一种兼具覆盖性和可审计性的验证架构。

Method: 将候选解重写为类型化状态转换序列，每个转换必须有明确理由（引用、计算或给定事实），并强制变更完备性，即所有状态差异都必须被解释，从而暴露隐藏前提。

Result: 在HLE-Verified Gold上，以91.4%精确度认证105/185问题；对抗性测试中捕捉94.7%毒化证明，远超整体评判的83.2%；在隐藏前提和捏造引用上优势显著。

Conclusion: Theoria通过结构化、可审计的验证实现了高精度认证，与LLM评判器互补，尤其擅长检测隐藏前提和捏造引用等关键错误类型。

中文摘要：何时应信任人工智能系统的答案？形式化证明辅助工具提供确定性，但无法覆盖大多数问题分布；标量LLM评判器提供覆盖性，但产生不透明的分数，事后无法审计，并且与任何LLM一样存在一致性问题。我们提出了Theoria，一种弥合这一差距的验证架构。候选解决方案被重写为一系列类型化状态转换，每个转换都有明确的理由，无论是引用、计算还是问题给定的事实，并且每个转换都可独立审计。基本不变量是变更的完备性：连续证明状态之间的每个差异都必须被解释，因此隐藏的前提会作为未经许可的突变出现，而不是无声地通过。在HLE-Verified Gold（185个纯文本专家问题）上，Theoria以91.4%的严格精确度认证了105个问题（Wilson 95% CI [84.5%, 95.4%]）。每个认证都会生成一个人类可读的证明轨迹，其中每一步都可以独立质疑。整体LLM评判器在匹配覆盖率下实现了相当的精确度，但在不同问题上失败（Jaccard指数0.14-0.36），使这些方法互补。在15个领域的95个对抗性毒化证明中，结构化评判器捕获了94.7%，而整体评判器为83.2%（p=0.0017）。总体11.5个百分点的差距集中在隐藏前提（90.6% vs. 62.5%，差距28个百分点）和捏造引用（100% vs. 90%）上，这些是形式化分析预测其优势的错误类别；在算术和定理误用错误上性能相同，这些领域未预测到优势。在GPQA Diamond（n=65）上，认证精确度为97.1%（Wilson CI [85.1%, 99.5%]）。

Original abstract: When should an AI system's answer be trusted? Formal proof assistants offer certainty but cannot reach most of the problem distribution; scalar LLM judges offer coverage but produce opaque scores that cannot be audited after the fact and are subject to the same coherence issues as any LLM. We present Theoria, a verification architecture that closes this gap. A candidate solution is rewritten into a sequence of typed state transitions, each licensed by an explicit justification, whether that be a citation, computation, or problem-given fact, and every transition is independently auditable. The foundational invariant is completeness of change: every difference between consecutive proof states must be accounted for, so hidden premises surface as unlicensed mutations rather than passing silently. On HLE-Verified Gold (185 text-only expert problems), Theoria certifies 105 at 91.4% strict precision (Wilson 95% CI [84.5%, 95.4%]). Every certification produces a human readable proof trace in which each step can be independently challenged. Holistic LLM judges achieve comparable precision at matched coverage but fail on different problems (Jaccard 0.14-0.36), making the approaches complementary. On 95 adversarial poisoned proofs across 15 domains, structured judges catch 94.7% versus 83.2% for holistic judging (p= 0.0017). The overall 11.5 pp gap concentrates in hidden premises (90.6% vs. 62.5%, a 28 pp difference) and fabricated citations (100% vs. 90%), the error classes where the formal analysis predicts an advantage; performance is identical on arithmetic and theorem-misapplication errors, where no advantage is predicted. On GPQA Diamond (n= 65), certified precision is 97.1% (Wilson CI [85.1%, 99.5%]).

</details>


### [60] [AutoMem: Automated Learning of Memory as a Cognitive Skill](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01224v1)
*Shengguang Wu,Hao Zhu,Yuhui Zhang,Xiaohan Wang,Serena Yeung-Levy*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出自动化内存管理作为agent可训练技能，显著提升长程任务性能，可迁移至coding agent。

TL;DR: AutoMem框架通过自动化内存结构优化和内存决策训练，将LLM的内存管理作为可学习技能，在长视野任务上实现约2-4倍性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长视野任务中内存管理依赖手动优化，但轨迹过长、错误隐蔽，难以人工审查，因此需要自动化方法。

Method: 提出AutoMem框架，包含两个循环：第一循环用强LLM审查完整轨迹并迭代修订内存结构；第二循环从多情节中识别良好内存决策作为训练信号，直接提升模型记忆熟练度。

Result: 在Crafter、MiniHack和NetHack三个游戏中，仅优化内存（不修改任务行为）使基础智能体性能提升约2-4倍，32B开放权重模型达到与Claude Opus 4.5和Gemini 3.1 Pro Thinking竞争的水平。

Conclusion: 内存管理是独立可学习的技能，是长视野任务的高杠杆优化目标，能带来显著性能增益。

中文摘要：记忆专长是一种习得的技能：知道要编码什么、何时检索以及如何组织知识——在认知科学中被称为元记忆的能力。我们将这一视角引入LLM，将内存管理视为一种可训练的技能。我们将文件系统操作提升为与任务操作同等的一级内存操作，让模型自己决定如何管理其内存。这种内存技能沿着两个轴提升：支持它的结构（提示、文件模式、操作词汇），以及运用它的模型的熟练度。这两个轴都难以手动优化：长视野任务中的情节运行数千步，一次内存错误可能在暴露出问题之前隐藏很长时间，使得人类审查完整轨迹不切实际。我们引入了AutoMem，一个自动化这两个轴的框架。在第一个循环中，一个强大的LLM审查完整的智能体轨迹，并迭代修订塑造智能体与其内存文件交互的内存结构。在第二个循环中，从许多情节中识别智能体自身良好的内存决策，并用作训练信号直接提高模型的记忆熟练度。在三个程序生成的长视野游戏（Crafter、MiniHack和NetHack）中，仅优化内存——而不修改模型的任务行动行为——将基础智能体的性能提高了约2-4倍，使一个32B开放权重模型能够与前沿系统如Claude Opus 4.5和Gemini 3.1 Pro Thinking竞争。我们的结果表明，内存管理是一种独立可学习的技能，并且是一个高杠杆的目标，在长视野任务上产生巨大收益。

Original abstract: Memory expertise is a learned skill: knowing what to encode, when to retrieve, and how to organize knowledge--a capacity known in cognitive science as metamemory. We bring this perspective to LLMs by treating memory management as a trainable skill. We promote file-system operations to first-class memory actions alongside task actions, letting the model itself decide how to manage its memory. This memory skill improves along two axes: the structure that supports it (prompts, file schemas, action vocabulary), and the proficiency of the model exercising it. Both axes resist manual optimization: episodes in long-horizon tasks run for thousands of steps, and a single memory mistake can hide long before it surfaces, making human review of full trajectories impractical. We introduce AutoMem, a framework that automates both axes. In the first loop, a strong LLM reviews complete agent trajectories and iteratively revises the memory structure that shapes how the agent interacts with its memory files. In the second loop, the agent's own good memory decisions are identified from many episodes and used as training signal to sharpen the model's memory proficiency directly. Across three procedurally generated long-horizon games (Crafter, MiniHack, and NetHack), optimizing memory alone--without modifying the model's task-action behavior--improved the base agent's performance ~2x-4x, bringing a 32B open-weight model competitive with frontier systems such as Claude Opus 4.5 and Gemini 3.1 Pro Thinking. Our results show that memory management is an independently learnable skill, and a high-leverage objective yielding large gains on long-horizon tasks.

</details>


### [61] [Auto-FL-Research: Agentic Search for Federated Learning Algorithms](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01366v1)
*Holger R. Roth,Ziyue Xu,Chester Chen,Daguang Xu,Peter Cnudde,Andrew Feng*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 基于agent的联邦学习算法搜索工作流，涉及代码生成与搜索，对agent驱动的自动优化有启发。

TL;DR: 提出了Auto-FL-Research (AFR)，一种约束编码代理工作流，用于自动搜索联邦学习算法配方，在多个任务上取得了一定改进，但结果混合，区分了真正的机制改进和表面调优效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 联邦学习研究中存在大量难以手动探索和公平比较的算法选择，需要自动化方法。

Method: 基于约束编码代理工作流AFR，代理可提出并实现候选训练算法，包括聚合规则、更新计划、目标函数和模型变体，由任务配置文件固定超参数和评估方式。

Result: 在多个医疗和LEAF任务上，AFR在部分任务上取得进展，但有些改进是表面调优或偶发结果，对照组分析揭示了不同来源。

Conclusion: AFR能自动搜索FL算法配方并发现有效机制，但需谨慎区分真正改进与调优效应，混合结果本身就是贡献。

中文摘要：联邦学习（FL）研究通常依赖于许多微小但重要的算法选择：优化器变体、服务器聚合规则、本地训练计划、归一化、正则化和模型架构。这些选择手动探索成本高，且当候选更改也可能改变FL训练或评估路径时，难以公平比较。在这项工作中，我们提出了Auto-FL-Research（AFR），一种用于FL算法配方搜索的约束编码代理工作流。代理可以提出并实现候选训练算法，包括服务器聚合规则、客户端更新计划、本地目标和注册模型变体，而任务配置文件固定突变表面、计算预算、通信合同和最终模型评估。每次实验记录候选分数、运行时间、编辑文件、工件和失败状态。我们在五个医疗跨机构FLamby任务和五个固定LEAF数据集加上LEAF合成任务的分组客户端配置文件上评估了AFR。五种子重复评估支持在四个FLamby任务和六个LEAF配置文件中的五个上取得进展，同时也暴露了种子敏感和搜索选择的失败案例。相同预算的对照显示，一些进展对应FL配方更改，而其他改进由固定表面标量控制恢复，或在重复或留出评估中失败。这些混合结果是贡献的一部分：它们展示了如何将代理生成的候选分离为重复的FL机制、固定表面调整效果和选择性的单次运行伪影。

Original abstract: Federated learning (FL) research often depends on many small but consequential algorithmic choices: optimizer variants, server aggregation rules, local training schedules, normalization, regularization, and model architecture. These choices are expensive to explore manually and difficult to compare fairly when candidate changes can also alter the FL training or evaluation path. In this work, we present Auto-FL-Research (AFR), a constrained coding-agent workflow for FL algorithmic recipe search. Agents may propose and implement candidate training algorithms, including server aggregation rules, client update schedules, local objectives, and registered model variants, while task profiles fix the mutation surface, compute budget, communication contract, and final model evaluation. Each campaign records candidate scores, runtime, edited files, artifacts, and failure status. We evaluate AFR on five healthcare cross-silo FLamby tasks and on grouped-client profiles for the five fixed LEAF datasets plus the LEAF synthetic task. Five-seed repeat evaluations support gains on four FLamby tasks and five of six LEAF profiles, while also exposing seed-sensitive and search-selected failure cases. Same-budget controls show that several gains correspond to FL-recipe changes, whereas other improvements are recovered by fixed-surface scalar controls or fail under repeat or held-out evaluation. These mixed outcomes are part of the contribution: they show how agent-generated candidates can be separated into repeated FL mechanisms, fixed-surface tuning effects, and selected single-run artifacts.

### [62] [Agent4cs: A Multi-agent System for Code Summarization in Large Hierarchical Codebases](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01425v2)
*Yongjian Tang,Ezgi Sarikayak,Doruk Tuncel,Jie M. Zhang,Thomas Runkler*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent代码摘要框架，直接涉及coding agent与代码理解。

TL;DR: Agent4cs是一个多智能体框架，通过自底向上的方式总结大型代码库，在7个模型上平均提升语义一致性8%，关键词覆盖率提升高达38%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代码摘要方法将源代码视为平面文本，未充分利用仓库的层次结构和依赖关系，且依赖单一模型，难以处理大型复杂代码库。

Method: 提出Agent4cs多智能体框架，包含三个智能体：总结智能体生成稳健摘要、关键词提取智能体识别子文件夹关键信息、质量保证智能体迭代优化输出，以自底向上方式工作。

Result: 在7个前沿模型上，与两个结构化提示基线相比，Agent4cs在所有文件夹级别平均提升语义一致性8%；在真实数据集上，归一化关键词覆盖率提升高达38%。

Conclusion: Agent4cs通过多智能体协作和自底向上策略，显著提升了大型代码库摘要的语义一致性和关键词覆盖率，优于现有基线方法。

中文摘要：理解大型、复杂的代码库，尤其是那些具有混淆结构和不完整文档的代码库，仍然是一个重大挑战。现有的代码摘要解决方案通常依赖于单一语言模型或编码助手（如Claude Code），并将源代码视为平面文本，未充分利用仓库中的丰富依赖关系和层次结构信息。为了解决这些不足，我们提出了Agent4cs——一个多智能体框架，以自底向上的方式总结大型代码库，其中总结智能体专注于生成稳健的摘要；关键词提取智能体主动识别子文件夹中的关键信息；质量保证智能体迭代地优化输出，以提高可读性、连贯性和完整性。在7个前沿模型上的评估表明，与两个使用代码片段的结构化提示基线相比，Agent4cs在所有文件夹级别的语义一致性上平均提高了8%。此外，在真实世界数据集上的广泛评估显示，与相同基线相比，归一化关键词覆盖率提高了高达38%。

Original abstract: Understanding large, complex codebases, especially those with obfuscated structures and incomplete documentation, remains a significant challenge. Existing code summarization solutions often rely on a single language model or coding assistant like Claude Code, and treat source code as flat text, underutilizing the rich interdependencies and hierarchical information within a repository. To address these shortcomings, we propose Agent4cs - a multi-agent framework that summarizes large codebases in a bottom-up fashion, where a summarization agent focuses on producing robust summaries; a keyword-extraction agent proactively identifies critical information from subfolders; and a quality-assurance agent iteratively refines the outputs for readability, coherence, and completeness. Evaluated on 7 frontier models, Agent4cs improves semantic consistency across all folder levels by average 8% compared to two structured prompting baselines with code segments. Furthermore, extensive evaluation on real-world datasets demonstrates up to 38% gains in normalized keyword coverage rate over the same baselines.
