### [63] [When Should Service Agents Reconsider? Difficulty-Routed Control in Customer-Service Operations](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01426v1)
*Qian Chen,Chengyuan Liu,Xin Yu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 服务agent的难度路由控制架构，可迁移至coding agent的错误预防与验证。

TL;DR: 提出一种难度导向的服务控制架构，通过轻量级路由器将常规会话与操作耦合会话分离，并在升级路径中使用冲突感知通信和写入触发的重新考虑，以提高客户服务代理执行后端写操作时的可靠性和效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主客户服务代理从对话转向操作执行，需要在保持常规服务快速低摩擦的同时，防止操作错误，尤其是在客户指令、策略、记录和写入交互时。

Method: 设计难度导向服务控制架构：轻量级路由器将常规会话保持在低成本基线路径，将操作耦合会话路由到升级工作流；升级路径采用冲突感知通信和写入触发的重新考虑，在重要写入前集中审议。

Result: 在零售任务中，该方法在操作冲突请求上可靠性持续提升；路由显示强控制针对冲突请求而非常规请求；增加的轮次和工具调用支持证据收集等，而非无差别扩展；案例显示升级工作流保留后备计划等。在航空任务上扩展了相同逻辑。

Conclusion: 难度导向服务控制架构能有效区分常规与操作耦合会话，通过针对性控制提升可靠性，不依赖无差别扩展，可扩展至不同领域。

中文摘要：自主客户服务代理正在从对话界面转向操作执行角色：它们检索企业记录、应用服务策略并执行后端写入操作，例如退款、取消、换货、订单修改和预订变更。这种转变带来了服务控制问题：企业必须保持常规服务快速且低摩擦，同时防止在客户指令、策略约束、企业记录和后端写入交互的请求上出现操作错误。我们提出了一种难度导向的服务控制架构，该架构询问服务代理在行动前何时应重新考虑。轻量级路由器将常规会话保持在低成本基线路径上，并将操作耦合的会话路由到升级的工作流。升级路径使用冲突感知通信和写入触发的重新考虑，在后果性的后端写入之前集中审议和保障措施，而不是对所有服务会话统一应用额外的控制。我们在来自τ²基准测试的人工验证的零售和航空任务上评估了该架构。在零售中，该方法在具有操作冲突的服务请求上持续提高了可靠性。路由证据表明，更强的控制针对冲突请求，而非广泛应用于常规请求。对话和工具使用概况表明，收益并非来自无差别的交互扩展或更广泛的工具链；相反，增加的轮次和工具调用支持了证据收集、写入分离和写入前重新考虑。案例级证据表明，升级的工作流保留了后备计划，将检索到的记录绑定到正确的操作，对写入进行排序，并分解了多实体请求。航空结果将相同的服务控制逻辑扩展到预订操作。

Original abstract: Autonomous customer-service agents are shifting from conversational interfaces toward operational execution roles: they retrieve firm records, apply service policies, and execute backend writes such as refunds, cancellations, exchanges, order modifications, and reservation changes. This shift creates a service-control problem: firms must keep routine service fast and low-friction while preventing operational errors on requests where customer instructions, policy constraints, firm records, and backend writes interact. We propose a difficulty-routed service-control architecture that asks when service agents should reconsider before acting. A lightweight router keeps routine sessions on a low-cost baseline path and routes operationally coupled sessions to an escalated workflow. The escalated path uses conflict-aware communication and write-triggered reconsideration to concentrate deliberation and safeguards before consequential backend writes, rather than applying additional control uniformly across all service sessions. We evaluate the architecture on human-verified retail and airline tasks from $τ^{2}$-bench. In retail, the method improves reliability consistently on service requests with operational conflict. Routing evidence shows that stronger control is directed toward conflicted requests rather than broadly applied to routine ones. Dialogue and tool-use profiles suggest that gains do not come from indiscriminate interaction expansion or broader tool chains; instead, added turns and tool calls support evidence gathering, write separation, and pre-write reconsideration. Case-level evidence shows that the escalated workflow preserves fallback plans, binds retrieved records to the correct action, sequences writes, and decomposes multi-entity requests. Airline results extend the same service-control logic to reservation operations.

### [64] [Beyond Next-Token Prediction: An RLVR Proof of Concept for Tool-Use Agents on Atlassian Workflows](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01465v1)
*Karthikeya Aditya Vissa,Sankalp Mane,Ananya Mantravadi,Harshit Rajgarhia,Abhishek Mukherji*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 利用RLVR训练工具使用agent，直接对应通用agent工具使用与RL方法，可迁移至coding agent。

TL;DR: 通过可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）直接在目标环境中训练小模型，在模拟Jira/Confluence API的五个合成场景中，RL训练将平均奖励从基线0.35-0.92提升至0.95-1.00，但手工奖励设计难以扩展，且部分场景基线已饱和。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在利基型企业SaaS工作流中存在目标不匹配（预测下一个词元 vs. 正确调用API），导致静默失败；RLVR可能弥合这一差距。

Method: 构建五个合成Jira/Confluence API环境，使用完全基于工具调用轨迹的可验证奖励，通过GRPO训练Qwen3-1.7B和Qwen3.5-4B模型。

Result: 在四个非退化场景中，RL训练将平均奖励从0.35-0.92提升至0.95-1.00，Confluence页面创建场景提升最大（0.35→1.00）；一个场景（工单转换）基线已饱和，RL无效。

Conclusion: RLVR可有效优化小模型在利基API上的表现，但手工奖励设计不可扩展，且部分场景无需RL即可达到最优。

中文摘要：大型语言模型被训练用于预测下一个词元，而不是在特定API内执行操作。在利基型企业SaaS工作流中——成功意味着以正确的顺序、使用正确的嵌套参数命中正确的端点——这种目标不匹配表现为静默失败：缺失必填字段、虚构工具，或在单次读取后提前停止。我们探究了直接应用于目标环境中的可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）是否能弥合这一差距。作为概念验证，我们构建了五个模拟Jira REST v3和Confluence v2 API的合成环境，保持模式保真度；奖励完全基于工具调用轨迹计算，无需实时API、无需学习型评判器、无需人工标注。使用驱动GRPO训练的相同检查器对提示后的Qwen3-1.7B和Qwen3.5-4B进行评分，我们发现，在四个奖励非退化的场景中，经过RL训练的策略将平均奖励从4B基线范围的0.35-0.92提升至0.95-1.00，其中Confluence页面创建场景的提升最大（0.35→1.00）。我们将此定位为针对利基型企业API的面向结果优化的小模型的前期步骤，并提出了两个研讨会读者应权衡的局限性：手工构建可验证奖励无法扩展到此处报告的少数端点之外，并且我们的五个场景之一（工单转换）具有饱和奖励形状，提示后的4B模型已经达到了最大值。

Original abstract: Large language models are trained to predict the next token, not to act inside a specific API. In niche enterprise SaaS workflows -- where success means hitting the right endpoint with the right nested arguments in the right order -- this objective mismatch shows up as silent failures: dropped required fields, hallucinated tools, or early stops after a single read. We ask whether Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR), applied directly in the target environment, closes the gap. As a proof of concept we build a suite of five synthetic environments emulating the Jira REST v3 and Confluence v2 APIs at schema fidelity; rewards are computed entirely from the tool-call trace, with no live API, no learned judge, and no human label in the loop. Scoring prompted Qwen3-1.7B and Qwen3.5-4B on the same checkers that drive GRPO training, we find that on the four scenarios whose rewards are non-degenerate the RL-trained policy lifts average reward from a 4B-baseline range of 0.35--0.92 to 0.95--1.00, with the largest single gain on Confluence page creation ($0.35 \rightarrow 1.00$). We position this as a preliminary step toward outcome-optimised small models for niche enterprise APIs, and foreground two limitations a workshop reader should weigh: hand-crafting verifiable rewards does not scale beyond the handful of endpoints reported here, and one of our five scenarios (ticket-transition) has a saturating reward shape that the prompted 4B already maxes out.

### [65] [World Feedback for Clinical Agents: Diagnosing RL in FHIR Environments](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01470v1)
*Ananya Mantravadi,Harshit Rajgarhia,Prasanna Desikan,Abhishek Mukherji*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 分析临床agent中RL的可学习性障碍，提出可迁移的诊断框架，对通用agent设计有启发。

TL;DR: MedAgentBench v3暴露了RL在临床任务中的两个结构性障碍（能力上限和格式-知识障碍），纯RL性能远低于SFT，分类法指导了混合修复策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 临床协议执行任务适合RL，但现有基准MedAgentBench v1/v2存在静默完成上限导致RL无效，需要构建新基准并分析RL的失败原因。

Method: 构建MedAgentBench-v3（508任务，8.9%上限），在Qwen3-8B上对比纯RL和基于规则的SFT，通过分类法分析任务类型。

Result: 纯RL pass@1为18.2%，SFT为34.1%，差距15.9个百分点；发现10/20任务类型无基础性能，3/20需要不可探索的临床代码。

Conclusion: RL受限于能力上限和格式-知识障碍，需用SFT注入代码知识，用RL学习条件逻辑，分类法可预测RL的可学习性。

中文摘要：临床协议执行任务——检查化验值、应用阈值、下达结构正确的FHIR医嘱——是从世界反馈中进行强化学习（RL）的自然候选：一旦临床领域专家将决策逻辑编码到验证器中，该验证器即可对无限次展开进行评分，无需每轮标注。但应用RL需要合理的反馈通道和足够的基础能力。我们审查了MedAgentBench v1/v2，发现存在41.7%的静默完成上限，使得不作为成为RL的占优策略，并构建了**MedAgentBench-v3 (MAB-v3)**（508个任务，8.9%上限）。训练Qwen3-8B暴露了两个结构性障碍：*能力上限*（10/20的任务类型基础性能为0%，梯度为零）和*格式-知识障碍*（3/20的类型需要精确的临床代码，无法通过探索发现）。纯RL达到18.2%的pass@1，而基于规则的SFT达到34.1%；15.9个百分点的差距完全可归因于这些障碍。一个决策/格式-知识/查找分类法预测了RL的可学习性，并规定了修复方法：SFT注入代码，RL学习条件判断。

Original abstract: Clinical protocol-execution tasks -- checking a lab value, applying a threshold, placing a correctly structured FHIR order -- are natural candidates for RL from world feedback: once clinical SMEs encode decision logic into a verifier, that verifier grades unlimited rollouts without per-episode annotation. But applying RL requires a sound feedback channel and sufficient base capability. We audit MedAgentBench v1/v2, find a 41.7\% silent-finish ceiling that makes inaction the RL dominant strategy, and construct \textbf{MedAgentBench-v3 (MAB-v3)} (508 tasks, 8.9\% ceiling). Training Qwen3-8B exposes two structural barriers: a \emph{capability ceiling} (10/20 task types have 0\% base performance, zero gradient) and a \emph{format-knowledge barrier} (3/20 types require exact clinical codes undiscoverable by exploration). Pure RL reaches 18.2\% pass@1 vs.\ 34.1\% for rule-based SFT; the 15.9~pp gap is attributable entirely to these barriers. A decision/format-knowledge/lookup taxonomy predicts RL learnability and prescribes the fix: SFT to inject codes, RL to learn conditionals.

### [66] [Procedural Memory Distillation: Online Reflection for Self-Improving Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01480v1)
*Ye Liu,Srijan Bansal,Bo Pang,Yang Li,Zeyu Leo Liu,Yifei Ming,Zixuan Ke,Shafiq Joty,Semih Yavuz*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出过程记忆蒸馏用于自我改进，在LiveCodeBench上评估，直接涉及coding agent的自我提升方法。

TL;DR: PMD通过将跨回合的程序性信号蒸馏为策略权重，使模型在推理时无需记忆，在多个基准上显著优于SDPO。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RLVR和SDPO方法仅使用回合级别的信号，忽略了rollout中的过程信息，无法利用跨回合的重复模式。

Method: 提出程序性记忆蒸馏（PMD），在三个抽象层次（原始轨迹、自我反思策略、高级行为模式）在线提取记忆，并通过记忆条件化的自我教师监督学生，实现记忆与策略的共同进化。

Result: 在Qwen3-8B和OLMo3-Instruct-7B上，PMD在SCIKNOWEVAL上提升3.8-5.5%，在LIVECODEBENCH上提升7.9-13.6%；共同进化是关键，冻结记忆或策略导致性能下降超10%。

Conclusion: PMD有效地将跨回合的过程性知识内化到策略中，无需推理时额外记忆，显著提升性能，且共同进化设计不可或缺。

中文摘要：带可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）以及最近的自我蒸馏变体（如SDPO）会根据验证器评估每次 rollout，并根据该回合级别的信号更新策略。然而，rollout 中更丰富的过程信息很少被保留或重用。在多个回合和多个训练周期中，模型在不断变化的策略下反复遇到相关问题，从而产生回合局部更新无法捕获的跨回合信号：哪些策略始终通过验证，哪些失败模式持续存在，哪些模式反复出现。我们提出程序性记忆蒸馏（PMD），它将这些跨回合信号转换为可重用的程序性记忆，并在训练期间将其蒸馏到策略的权重中。这种记忆充当训练支架，被策略本身吸收，从而在推理时产生无记忆模型。PMD 在三个抽象层次组织记忆：原始轨迹、自我反思的策略和经验，以及跨问题重复出现的高级行为模式，所有这些都从模型自身的轨迹中在线提取。一个由记忆条件化的自我教师利用累积的经验来监督学生在其自身 rollout 上的表现，使学生能够逐步将程序性知识内化到其参数中。核心设计原则是共同进化：策略生成 rollout 以更新记忆，而记忆塑造监督以更新策略。实验上，在 Qwen3-8B 和 OLMo3-Instruct-7B 上，PMD 在 SCIKNOWEVAL 上比 SDPO 提高了 3.8-5.5%，在 LIVECODEBENCH 上提高了 7.9-13.6%。共同进化驱动了这些增益：在 SCIKNOWEVAL 领域上，冻结记忆或策略都会使 PMD 落后超过 10%。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR), along with recent selfdistillation variants such as SDPO, evaluates each rollout against a verifier and updates the policy from that episode-level signal. However, the richer procedural information in the rollout is rarely retained or reused. Across episodes and epochs, the model repeatedly encounters related problems under a changing policy, producing cross-episode signals that episode-local updates cannot capture: which strategies consistently pass verification, which failure modes persist, which patterns recur. We propose Procedural Memory Distillation (PMD), which converts these crossepisode signals into reusable procedural memory and distills it into the policy's weights during training. This memory functions as a training scaffold, absorbed into the policy itself, yielding a memory-free model at inference. PMD organizes the memory at three levels of abstraction: raw trajectories, self-reflected strategies and lessons, and higher-level behavioral patterns that recur across problems, all extracted online from the model's own trajectories. A memory-conditioned self-teacher draws on the accumulated experience to supervise the student on its own rollouts, enabling student to progressively internalize procedural knowledge within its parameters. The central design principle is co-evolution: the policy generates rollouts that update the memory, and memory shapes the supervision that updates the policy. Empirically, across Qwen3-8B and OLMo3-Instruct-7B, PMD improves over SDPO by 3.8-5.5% on SCIKNOWEVAL and 7.9-13.6% on LIVECODEBENCH. Co-evolution powers these gains: freezing either the memory or the policy trails PMD by more than 10% across SCIKNOWEVAL domains.

</details>


### [67] [The Agentic Garden of Forking Paths](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01507v1)
*Jiacheng Miao,Jonathan K Pritchard,James Zou*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出agent多值分析框架，用于评估agent分析的可信度，对agent评测有一般贡献。

TL;DR: 研究表明，AI代理可以模拟人类研究人员因不同分析选择得出的分歧结论，并引入m-value和Agentic Bootstrap方法来评估分析路径的极端性，从而解决选择性探索和报告的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实证研究中不同分析选择可能导致不同结论，但这些隐藏的分叉路径难以观察。AI代理可以揭示这些路径，但可能放大选择性探索的问题。需要一种方法来量化分析路径的极端性并评估科学证据的可靠性。

Method: 通过分配不同角色给AI代理，使其从相同数据得出不同结论；引入m-value（分析路径产生至少与报告一样极端结果的条件概率）和Agentic Bootstrap（用AI代理采样分析路径以估计m-value）。

Result: AI代理再现了人类研究团队72%的意识形态差距；86%的AI报告通过独立AI审查，78%通过人类专家审查；13.5%的人类分析落在最极端5%的分析空间中（m<0.05）。

Conclusion: 科学证据应基于分析分布而非单一分析来评估；Agentic Bootstrap使分布可观察，可作为科学可信度的标准。

中文摘要：实证研究很少承认唯一分析。不同的分析选择可能导致从相同数据得出不同结论，然而这些隐藏的分叉路径很难被观察到。我们展示了AI代理能够捕捉人类研究人员之间的许多分析变异，同时使这些路径变得明确。在四个高风险领域，分配不同的角色足以让AI代理从相同数据和问题中报告出不同的、常常是对立的结论，且发现与这些信念系统性地一致。在一项42个人类研究团队分析相同移民数据集的研究中，AI代理再现了人类在报告效应估计中72%的意识形态差距。尽管得出对立结论，但基于最终AI报告很难识别每个分析中的明确问题：86%通过了独立AI审查，78%通过了多数人类专家审查。这些发现表明，核心挑战往往不是有缺陷的分析，而是从大量方法上可辩护的分析空间中进行选择性探索和报告。AI代理可能通过使这种探索变得廉价和可扩展来放大这个长期存在的问题。为了解决这个问题，我们引入了m-value（多宇宙值），即一个分析路径产生至少与报告一样极端的主张的概率。我们进一步引入了Agentic Bootstrap，它通过使用AI代理对可能的分析路径进行抽样来估计m-value。应用于人类移民研究，13.5%的报告人类分析落在分析空间中最极端的5%中（m<0.05）。因此，科学证据不仅应该根据单一报告的分析来评估，还应该根据其在合理报告的分布中的位置来评估。Agentic Bootstrap使这个分布变得可观察，并将其转化为科学可信度的标准。

Original abstract: Empirical research rarely admits a unique analysis. Different analytical choices can lead to different conclusions from the same data, yet these hidden forking paths are difficult to observe. We show that AI agents capture much of the analytical variation among human researchers while making these paths explicit. Across four high-stakes domains, assigning different personas is sufficient for AI agents to report divergent, often opposing, conclusions from the same data and question, with findings systematically aligned with those beliefs. In a study in which 42 human research teams analyzed the same immigration dataset, AI agents reproduced 72% of the human ideological gap in reported effect estimates. Despite reaching opposing conclusions, it is difficult to identify clear issues in each analysis based on the final AI reports: 86% passed independent AI review and 78% passed majority human expert review. These findings suggest that the central challenge is often not flawed analyses, but selective exploration and reporting from a large space of methodologically defensible analyses. AI agents may amplify this longstanding problem by making such exploration inexpensive and scalable. To address this, we introduce the m-value (multiverse value), the probability that an analysis path would produce a claim at least as extreme as the reported one. We further introduce Agentic Bootstrap, which estimates the m-value by using AI agents to sample plausible analysis paths. Applied to the human immigration study, 13.5% of reported human analyses fell in the most extreme 5% of the analysis space (m<0.05). Scientific evidence should therefore be evaluated not only by a single reported analysis but also by its position within the distribution of analyses that could reasonably have been reported. Agentic Bootstrap makes this distribution observable and turns it into a criterion for scientific credibility.

</details>


### [68] [Janus: a Playground for User-Involved Agentic Permission Management](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01510v1)
*Natalie Grace Brigham,Eugene Bagdasarian,Tadayoshi Kohno,Franziska Roesner*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出agent权限管理平台，涉及多agent系统与用户交互设计，可迁移至coding agent安全。

TL;DR: Janus是一个用于实现和评估用户参与式代理权限管理的系统，通过六个权限助手在多个场景下的评估，发现用户输入对隐私安全至关重要，AI可减轻认知负担，但无单一设计适用于所有情境。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI代理自主执行工具调用引发权限管理问题，用户角色未充分探索，需要系统化研究用户参与式权限管理设计。

Method: 开发了Janus系统，包含模块化代理系统Janus-Core和自动化评估框架Janus-Harness；基于概念模型设计六个权限助手，在三个场景和三个合成响应者上进行评估。

Result: 用户输入显著增强隐私安全；AI增强可降低认知负荷；需考虑现实用户行为如权限疲劳；无单一设计普遍最优。

Conclusion: 应采用更原则性和上下文敏感的权限管理设计，Janus开源支持后续研究。

中文摘要：AI代理在用户授权下自主执行工具调用，引发了关于权限管理的紧迫问题：用户可能扮演什么角色，应该扮演什么角色？尽管提出了许多方法，用户参与式的代理权限管理仍待深入探索。我们介绍了Janus，一个用于实现和评估用户参与式代理权限管理设计的游乐场系统。Janus包含两个组件：Janus-Core，一个支持多种权限管理设计的模块化代理系统；以及Janus-Harness，一个自动化评估框架。基于一个识别用户参与关键设计轴的概念模型，我们实现了覆盖设计空间的六个权限助手，并在三个场景和三个合成响应者上进行了评估。我们证明用户输入至关重要，能显著增强隐私和安全性；AI增强用户决策有助于减轻认知负担；系统设计必须考虑现实用户行为（包括权限疲劳）。没有单一设计在所有情境下表现最优，这激励在代理系统中部署权限助手时采用更原则性且上下文敏感的方法。Janus已公开可用，以支持未来对这一代理系统设计维度的研究。

Original abstract: AI agents that autonomously execute tool calls on a user's behalf raise pressing questions about permission management: what role could users play, and what role should they play? Despite many proposed approaches, the user's role in agentic permission management remains under explored. We introduce Janus, a playground system for implementing and evaluating user-involved agentic permission management designs. Janus consists of two components: Janus-Core, a modular agentic system supporting a diverse spectrum of permission management designs, and Janus-Harness, an automated evaluation framework. Grounded in a conceptual model that identifies key design axes for user involvement, we implement six permission assistants spanning the design space and evaluate them across three scenarios and three synthetic responders. We demonstrate that user input is critical and can significantly strengthen privacy and security, that AI augmentation of user decisions can help reduce cognitive load, and that realistic user behavior including permission fatigue must be accounted for in system design. No single design performs optimally across all contexts, motivating a more principled and context-sensitive approach to deploying permission assistants in agentic systems. Janus is publicly available to support future investigation into this dimension of agentic system design.

</details>


### [69] [OPINE-World: Programmatic World Modeling with Ontology-error-Prioritized Interactive Exploration for ARC-AGI-3](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01531v2)
*David Courtis,Wenhao Li,Scott Sanner*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM agent在线学习程序化世界模型，涉及探索与程序合成，可迁移至自动化代码优化中的world modeling。

TL;DR: OPINE-World是一个LLM智能体，通过交互在线学习以对象为中心的程序化世界模型，在ARC-AGI-3基准上实现了高效技能获取，无需每游戏训练即可解决大多数游戏。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有世界模型方法存在数据效率低或可扩展性差的问题，需要一种既能高效学习又能适应像素渲染环境的世界模型学习方法。

Method: OPINE-World通过两个协作智能体（行动者和合成者）在假设-测试循环中工作，行动者探索环境，合成者用代码构建世界模型，并通过回放验证和基于模型的规划进行精炼，同时使用本体误差贝叶斯度量引导探索。

Result: 在ARC-AGI-3基准上，OPINE-World在无需每游戏训练的情况下解决了25个游戏中的20个，动作效率分数为78.4，接近人类基线。

Conclusion: OPINE-World展示了在线学习以对象为中心的程序化世界模型的有效性，在技能获取效率上取得了显著成果，为适应不熟悉任务的智能体构建提供了新方向。

中文摘要：通过交互学习环境的行为是构建适应不熟悉任务的智能体的核心。使用深度网络学习的世界模型灵活但数据需求大，并且在其训练分布之外迁移性差。由LLM编写源代码并通过反例引导归纳合成（CEGIS）精炼的程序合成世界模型则是数据高效且可重复使用的，但它们主要被展示在具有给定对象词汇的结构化状态世界中，而单一程序搜索无法扩展到像素渲染环境中，因为其对象结构必须灵活地假设。我们介绍了OPINE-World，一个LLM智能体，它通过交互在线学习以对象为中心的程序化世界模型。OPINE-World在假设与测试的循环中耦合了两个协作的智能体，一个在环境中行动，另一个用代码合成模型，并进行回放验证和基于模型的规划，并通过我们称为本体误差的对象类型充分性的贝叶斯度量来引导探索。我们在ARC-AGI-3上评估OPINE-World，这是一个技能获取效率的基准，其中对象词汇、目标和动作语义都被隐藏。OPINE-World在无需每游戏训练的情况下解决了25个游戏中的20个，并达到了78.4的动作效率分数，与人类基线相比。

Original abstract: Learning how an environment behaves from interaction is central to building agents that adapt to unfamiliar tasks. World models learned with deep networks are flexible but data-hungry and transfer poorly beyond their training distribution. Program-synthesized world models, written as source code by LLMs and refined through counterexample-guided inductive synthesis (CEGIS), are instead data-efficient and reusable, yet they have been demonstrated mainly on structured-state worlds with a given object vocabulary, and a single program search does not scale to pixel-rendered environments whose object structure must be hypothesized flexibly. We introduce OPINE-World, an LLM agent that learns an object-centric programmatic world model online from interaction. OPINE-World couples two cooperating agents in a loop of hypothesis and test, one acting in the environment and one synthesizing the model in code with replay verification and model-based planning, and it steers exploration with a Bayesian measure of object-type adequacy we call ontology error. We evaluate OPINE-World on ARC-AGI-3, a benchmark for skill-acquisition efficiency in which the object vocabulary, the goal, and the action semantics are withheld. OPINE-World solves 20 of 25 games without per-game training and reaches an action-efficiency score of 78.4 against the human baseline.

</details>

### [70] [Exploring the Semantic Gap in Agentic Data Systems: A Formative Study of Operationalization Failures in Analytical Workflows](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00828v1)
*Jalal Mahmud,Eser Kandogan*

Main category: cs.DB

Selection reason: 研究Agentic数据系统的操作化失败，对Coding Agent的鲁棒性设计有通用启发

TL;DR: LLM生成的分析工作流中存在五类操作化失败，源于用户概念与系统信息之间的语义鸿沟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示LLM生成的分析工作流中操作化失败的普遍类型及其根本原因，以指导更智能的语义表示系统设计。

Method: 跨领域形成性研究，分析236个分析意图及其工作流生成与执行结果，识别重复失败模式。

Result: 识别出五类重复失败：比较基础、过程推理、定量推理、角色混淆和政策基础，共153个实例。

Conclusion: 存在语义鸿沟，未来智能体数据系统需要更丰富的语义表示以连接分析意图与可执行计算。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）越来越多地被用于生成查询、调用工具和构建分析工作流。尽管最近的进展显著改善了工作流的生成和执行，但操作化分析概念所需的语义信息往往超出了数据库模式和数据值中显式表示的内容。我们提出了一项跨领域的形成性研究，关于智能体生成的分析工作流中的操作化失败。在涵盖金融、人力资源和公共安全领域的236个分析意图中，我们识别出153个重复出现的失败，尽管工作流生成和执行成功。我们的分析揭示了五类重复出现的失败：比较基础、过程推理、定量推理、角色混淆和政策基础。这些发现表明用户级分析概念与工作流生成系统可用信息之间存在语义鸿沟。更广泛地说，它们引发了对分析操作可接受性的质疑，并表明未来的智能体数据系统可能需要更丰富的语义表示来弥合分析意图与可执行计算之间的差距。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used to generate queries, invoke tools, and construct analytical workflows. Although recent advances have substantially improved workflow generation and execution, the semantic information required to operationalize analytical concepts often lies beyond what is explicitly represented in database schemas and data values. We present a cross-domain formative study of operationalization failures in agent-generated analytical workflows. Across 236 analytical intents spanning finance, human resources, and public safety domains, we identify 153 recurring failures despite successful workflow generation and execution. Our analysis reveals five recurring classes of failures: comparative grounding, process reasoning, quantitative reasoning, role confusion, and policy grounding. These findings suggest a semantic gap between user-level analytical concepts and the information available to workflow-generation systems. More broadly, they raise questions about the admissibility of analytical operations and suggest that future agentic data systems may require richer semantic representations to bridge the gap between analytical intent and executable computation.

### [71] [Mapping the Evaluation Frontier: An Empirical Survey of the Bias-Reliability Tradeoff Across Eleven Evaluator-Agent Conditions](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00304v1)
*Zewen Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 研究LLM评估系统的偏差-可靠性权衡，提出评估者耦合等度量，对agent评测有参考价值

TL;DR: 实验证实LLM评估系统中存在偏差-可靠性权衡：低评估器耦合导致高测量噪声，强耦合抑制策略多样性，且无法同时实现低耦合与低噪声。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前证据仅基于单一研究的少量条件，需要扩大实证基础验证偏差-可靠性权衡假设。

Method: 将条件数量扩展到11个，测量所有条件的gamma和H，对其中7个测量CV(N=5)，分析相关性并检查GPT-4o条件的异常模式。

Result: 低耦合条件(gamma<0.2)具有高噪声(CV>1.0)，强耦合条件(gamma>0.9)具有低噪声(CV<0.16)；相关性r=-0.989证实耦合抑制多样性；GPT-4o条件出现异常gamma=0和H=1；无条件同时满足低耦合和低噪声。

Conclusion: 数据确认了偏差-可靠性权衡，并揭示GPT-4o版本漂移问题；发布标准化基准数据集。

中文摘要：偏差-可靠性权衡假设LLM评估系统在(gamma, H, CV)空间中受到约束，其中评估器耦合度(gamma)、策略多样性(H)和小样本测量可靠性(CV(N))在固定样本量N下无法同时优化。先前的证据仅基于来自单一研究的n=5个条件及其完整指标。我们将经验基础扩展到11个条件，测量了所有11个条件的gamma和H（其中9个具有有效权重向量），以及7个具有足够种子(N>=5)条件的CV(N=5)。五个条件提供了完整的(gamma, H, CV)三元组。数据证实了这一权衡：低评估器耦合度(gamma<0.2)的条件表现出高测量噪声(CV(N=5)>1.0)，而强耦合度(gamma>0.9)的条件实现了低噪声(CV(N=5)<0.16)。相关性r(H, gamma)=-0.989 (n=5，排除GPT-4o条件)证实评估器耦合度抑制了策略多样性。四个GPT-4o条件在所有种子上显示gamma=0.000和H=1.000——我们将此模式归因于2026年6月GPT-4o API的版本漂移。没有条件占据{gamma<0.2, CV(N=5)<0.3}的区域。我们发布所有每个条件的指标，作为评估器比较的标准化基准数据集。

Original abstract: The bias-reliability tradeoff conjectures that LLM evaluation systems are constrained in (gamma, H, CV) space, where evaluator coupling (gamma), strategy diversity (H), and small-sample measurement reliability (CV(N)) cannot be simultaneously optimized at fixed sample size N. Prior evidence rests on n=5 conditions with complete metrics from a single study. We expand the empirical base to 11 conditions, measuring gamma and H for all 11 (nine with valid weight vectors) and CV(N=5) for seven with sufficient seeds (N >= 5). Five conditions provide the complete (gamma, H, CV) triple. The data confirm the trade-off: conditions with low evaluator coupling (gamma < 0.2) exhibit high measurement noise (CV(N=5) > 1.0), while conditions with strong coupling (gamma > 0.9) achieve low noise (CV(N=5) < 0.16). The correlation r(H, gamma) = -0.989 (n=5, excluding GPT-4o conditions) confirms that evaluator coupling suppresses strategy diversity. Four GPT-4o conditions show gamma=0.000 and H=1.000 across all seeds -- a pattern we attribute to version drift in the June 2026 GPT-4o API. No condition occupies the region {gamma < 0.2, CV(N=5) < 0.3}. We release all per-condition metrics as a standardized benchmark dataset for evaluator comparison.

</details>


### [72] [Auditing the Audit: Five Failure Modes in Benchmark-Validity Audits](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02586v1)
*Yanhang Li,Zhichao Fan,Zexin Zhuang*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 论文论证基于扰动的构念效度审计本身脆弱，结论可被实现细节悄然操控；通过六点门控检查，所有测试案例均未达到确认性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 治理框架依赖基于扰动的构念效度审计作为评估证据，但作者认为这类审计存在被实现细节操控的脆弱性，需要揭示和防范。

Method: 命名五类流水线故障（F1-F5），在安全基准和开放权重指令调优模型上执行自我审计，并应用统一的六点尽职调查门控进行评估。

Result: 在六点门控下，所有测试单元均落在非确认性区间，无一达到确认性。

Conclusion: 提出六点门控作为保证级证据的扣留和披露协议，补充而非替代经典构念效度证据，不用于基准效度判断。

中文摘要：治理框架要求AI提供者和审计师提供记录在案的评估证据，而基于扰动的构念效度审计是这类证据的常见形式。我们认为审计本身是脆弱的：其结论可能因实现细节而被悄然操控，而这些细节读者在报告的数字中无法看到。我们命名了五类流水线故障，并在安全基准和开放权重指令调优模型上的自我审计中展示了每一类。在一个统一的六点尽职调查门控下，每个单元均落在非确认性区间，没有单元达到确认性。这里的证据是一个单一的两模型、五基准案例研究，而F1-F5是一个说明性的、故意非穷尽的起点分类法——并非审计故障的全面划分。我们将该门控定位为对保证级证据的一种扣留和披露协议，是对经典构念效度证据的补充（而非替代），并且不是通往基准效度判断的路径。

Original abstract: Governance frameworks ask AI providers and auditors for documented evaluation evidence, and perturbation-based construct-validity audits are a common form of that evidence. We argue the audits are themselves fragile: their conclusions can be silently manufactured by implementation details that readers cannot see in the reported numbers. We name five classes of pipeline failure and demonstrate each in a self-audit over safety benchmarks and open-weight instruction-tuned models. Under a unified six-point due-diligence gate, every cell lands in a non-confirmatory bucket, and no cell reaches confirmatory. The evidence here is a single two-model, five-benchmark case study, and F1--F5 is an illustrative, deliberately non-exhaustive starting taxonomy -- not a comprehensive partition of audit failures. We position the gate as a withholding and disclosure protocol for assurance-grade evidence, supplementary to (not a replacement for) classical construct-validity evidence, and not as a route to benchmark-validity verdicts.

</details>


### [73] [Active-GRPO: Adaptive Imitation and Self-Improving Reasoning for Molecular Optimization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00531v1)
*Xuefeng Liu,Mingxuan Cao,Qinan Huang,Thomas Brettin,Rick Stevens,Le Cong*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: Active-GRPO强化学习方法，含自适应模仿与自我改进，可迁移至编码Agent的训练与策略优化。

TL;DR: 提出Active-GRPO方法，通过动态模仿与强化学习切换以及参考自动升级，在分子优化任务上显著提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法如SFT破坏推理、RLVR反馈稀疏，而参考引导策略优化受限于参考质量，需要突破性能上限。

Method: 提出主动推理范式，实例化为Active-GRPO，包含主动模仿-强化机制（根据参考与策略候选的相对优劣切换学习方式）和主动参考更新机制（用最优策略候选替换参考）。

Result: 在TOMG-Bench MOLOPT上，Active-GRPO的平均SRxSim达到0.1773，优于GRPO的0.0959和RePO的0.1665，且在LogP、MR、QED上统计显著。

Conclusion: Active-GRPO通过动态调整模仿与强化学习并持续升级参考，有效克服了参考质量限制，提升了分子优化中的科学推理能力。

中文摘要：科学推理是大语言模型日益重要的能力，然而提高训练此类推理的鲁棒性和效率仍然是一个关键开放挑战。我们在基于指令的分子优化中研究这个问题，其中仅答案的监督微调（SFT）会破坏多步推理，而带可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）则面临稀疏反馈问题。参考引导策略优化通过将策略更新锚定到数据集提供的参考来缓解这两个问题，但其效果与参考质量紧密相关：弱或不一致的参考会带来性能上限。为了突破这一上限，我们提出主动推理（active reasoning）范式，其中策略在每个实例上主动决定何时模仿参考以及何时强化自身的发现，同时持续升级其模仿的对象。我们将该范式实例化为主动组相对策略优化（Active-GRPO），通过两个耦合机制实现：主动模仿-强化和主动参考更新。前者在参考仍优于策略自身候选时执行模仿学习，一旦策略生成超越参考的分子，则转向通过强化学习进行自我改进。后者通过将参考替换为迄今为止发现的最佳策略生成候选来持续升级参考本身，逐步提高模仿目标，确保参考引导在整个训练过程中保持信息性而非限制性。在TOMG-Bench MOLOPT上，Active-GRPO在匹配的三次评估下将平均SRxSim从GRPO的0.0959和RePO的0.1665提升至0.1773，在LogP、MR和QED上具有统计显著性增益。

Original abstract: Scientific reasoning is an increasingly important capability of large language models, yet improving the robustness and efficiency of training such reasoning remains a key open challenge. We study this problem in instruction-based molecular optimization, where answer-only supervised fine-tuning (SFT) collapses multi-step reasoning and reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) suffers from sparse feedback. Reference-guided Policy Optimization mitigates both by anchoring policy updates to dataset-provided references, but its effectiveness is tightly coupled to reference quality: weak or misaligned references impose a performance ceiling. To overcome this ceiling, we propose active reasoning, a paradigm in which the policy actively decides, on a per-instance basis, when to imitate a reference and when to reinforce its own discoveries, while continuously upgrading what it imitates. We instantiate this paradigm as Active Group Relative Policy Optimization (Active-GRPO), realized through two coupled mechanisms: active imitate-reinforce and active referencing. The former performs imitation learning when the reference still outperforms the policy's own candidates, and shifts to self-improvement via reinforcement learning once the policy has generated molecules that surpass the reference. The latter continuously upgrades the reference itself by replacing it with the best policy-generated candidate discovered so far, progressively raising the imitation target and ensuring that reference guidance remains informative-rather than restrictive-throughout training. Across TOMG-Bench MOLOPT, Active-GRPO improves average SRxSim from 0.0959 for GRPO and 0.1665 for RePO to 0.1773 under matched three-seed evaluation, with statistically significant gains on LogP, MR, and QED.

</details>


### [74] [LLM-Guided ODE Discovery and Parameter Inference from Small-Cohort Aggregate Data](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00733v1)
*Hanning Yang,Meropi Karakioulaki,Lennart Purucker,Tim Litwin,Cristina Has,Moritz Hess*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: LLM引导的ODE发现与工具增强推理，架构可迁移至代码优化Agent

TL;DR: 本文提出AgentODE，一种仅从群体层面汇总统计联合发现ODE结构并细化参数分布的端到端框架，在罕见疾病数据上实现了功能一致的机制建模。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法无法仅从群体层面汇总统计联合发现ODE结构和估计参数分布，而罕见疾病中个体数据稀缺且有隐私限制，需要利用汇总统计进行机制建模。

Method: AgentODE利用LLM提出候选ODE结构，并通过工具增强的推理代理进行诊断-更新循环，仅基于群体层面汇总统计迭代优化参数分布。

Result: 在基准问题和临床数据集上，AgentODE恢复了功能一致的ODE结构；在RDEB上，利用汇总统计推理比利用个体数据的基线方法发现了更合理的结构。

Conclusion: AgentODE为数据稀缺和隐私受限的罕见疾病机制建模提供了新方法，可直接从群体汇总统计进行建模。

中文摘要：通过常微分方程（ODE）进行的机制建模为复杂动态提供了可解释的描述，并能够推断潜在机制，这在临床环境中尤为重要。然而，在罕见疾病中，模型的结构和参数通常都是未知的，而个体层面的数据稀缺、噪声大、异质性强，并受到隐私限制。在这种情况下，群体层面的汇总统计提供了一种实用的隐私保护数据表示，而捕捉异质性进一步需要将参数建模为分布而非固定值。然而，目前没有现有方法能够仅从汇总统计中联合发现ODE结构并细化参数分布。我们提出了AgentODE，一个端到端框架来解决这一空白。一个大型语言模型（LLM）提出候选的ODE结构，同时一个工具增强的推理代理通过诊断-更新循环迭代地细化参数分布，仅基于群体层面的汇总统计进行操作。我们在三个不同领域的基准问题以及两个临床数据集上评估了AgentODE，包括罕见疾病隐性营养不良性大疱性表皮松解症（RDEB），该数据集仅有46名患者的231个观测值。AgentODE在所有设置中恢复了功能一致的ODE结构，并且RDEB实验表明，在稀疏和噪声数据环境中，基于汇总统计的推理促进了基于机制的合理结构发现，而具有个体层面数据访问的基线方法尽管预测性能更好，却恢复了不合理的结构。AgentODE为直接从群体层面汇总统计进行罕见疾病的机制建模开辟了新的可能性，而数据稀缺和隐私限制传统上限制了此类分析。

Original abstract: Mechanistic modeling via ordinary differential equations (ODEs) provides interpretable descriptions of complex dynamics and enables inference of underlying mechanisms, which is particularly valuable in clinical settings. However, in rare diseases, both the structure and parameters of the model are typically unknown, while individual-level data is scarce, noisy, heterogeneous, and subject to privacy constraints. In such settings, population-level summary statistics provide a practical privacy-preserving data representation, while capturing heterogeneity further requires modeling parameters as distributions rather than fixed values. Yet no existing method jointly discovers ODE structure and refines parameter distributions solely from summary statistics. We present AgentODE, an end-to-end framework that addresses this gap. An LLM proposes candidate ODE structures, while a tool-augmented inference agent iteratively refines parameter distributions through a diagnosis--update loop, operating on population-level summary statistics alone. We evaluate AgentODE on three benchmark problems across different fields and two clinical datasets, including the rare disease recessive dystrophic epidermolysis bullosa (RDEB), with only 231 observations across 46 patients. AgentODE recovers functionally consistent ODE structures across all settings, and experiments on RDEB demonstrates that in sparse and noisy data settings reasoning from summary statistics promotes mechanistically principled structure discovery, whereas baselines with individual-level data access recover implausible structures despite better predictive performance. AgentODE opens new possibilities for mechanistic modeling of rare diseases directly from population-level summary statistics, where data scarcity and privacy constraints have traditionally limited such analyses.

### [75] [Staleness-Learning Rate Scaling Laws for Asynchronous RLHF](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01083v2)
*Jingwei Song,Haofeng Xu,Jie Xiao,Chengke Bao,Jingwei Shi,Pengbin Feng,Weixun Wang,Yuhang Han,Chuan Wu,Linfeng Zhang,Bill Shi*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 研究异步RLHF中陈旧性对学习率的影响，对Agent训练稳定性有可迁移的见解。

TL;DR: 研究了异步GRPO中过时rollout对策略优化的影响，推导了梯度偏差和稳定性条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高吞吐量RLHF系统中使用过时rollout可能导致学习不稳定，需要理论分析其影响。

Method: 在GRPO目标中显式建模行为策略，通过理论分析推导过时rollout引起的梯度偏差和稳定性条件。

Result: 过时rollout引入O(S*eta)的梯度偏差；稳定性条件为eta << min{R_batch/(S*G_upd), R_crit/(T*G_upd)}。

Conclusion: 过时rollout的影响可通过适当的学习率调整来控制，最大稳定学习率在水平有限范围内对过时性弱依赖。

中文摘要：高吞吐量RLHF系统通常将rollout生成与策略优化解耦，导致学习器更新时使用过时的rollout。在这项工作中，我们研究这种过时性在异步GRPO中的影响。我们将行为策略显式地纳入GRPO替代目标，并区分学习器使用的替代梯度映射和依赖于分布的种群目标的真实总导数。在局部有界性、分布平滑性和行为策略平滑性的假设下，我们证明过时rollout引入了阶数为O(S * eta)的每步替代梯度偏差，其中S表示最大rollout滞后，eta表示学习率。我们进一步推导出条件性的崩溃时间标度律：当周期内漂移保持低于批次级裁剪半径时，崩溃主要由累积学习器漂移T * eta控制；当过时rollout约束激活时，稳定性反而明确依赖于S * eta。这产生了一个双约束稳定性条件eta << min{R_batch / (S * G_upd), R_crit / (T * G_upd)}，解释了为什么在水平有限范围内，最大稳定学习率可能表现出对过时性的弱依赖性。

Original abstract: High-throughput RLHF systems often decouple rollout generation from policy optimization, leading to the use of stale rollouts during learner updates. In this work, we study the effect of such staleness in asynchronous GRPO. We make the behavior policy explicit in the GRPO surrogate objective and distinguish between the surrogate-gradient mapping used by the learner and the true total derivative of a distribution-dependent population objective. Under assumptions of local boundedness, distributional smoothness, and behavior-policy smoothness, we show that stale rollouts introduce a per-step surrogate-gradient bias of order O(S * eta), where S denotes the maximum rollout lag and eta denotes the learning rate. We further derive a conditional collapse-time scaling law: when within-cycle drift remains below a batch-level clipping radius, collapse is governed primarily by cumulative learner drift T * eta; when the stale-rollout constraint is active, stability instead depends explicitly on S * eta. This yields a two-constraint stability condition eta << min{R_batch / (S * G_upd), R_crit / (T * G_upd)}, explaining why the maximum stable learning rate may appear weakly dependent on staleness in the horizon-limited regime.

</details>


### [76] [Sequentially-Controlled Interactive Multi-Particle Flow-Maps for Online Feedback-Driven Search](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01144v1)
*Binglin Ji,Anindya Sarkar,Hengchang Lu,Jens Sjölund,Yevgeniy Vorobeychik*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 在线反馈驱动的多粒子搜索框架，可迁移至Agent偏好对齐与探索。

TL;DR: 提出一种序列控制交互式多粒子流图框架，通过后验样本共享和探索-利用重加权机制实现样本高效的在线反馈驱动搜索，在分布对齐任务中优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有生成模型的奖励对齐方法在偏好未知且仅通过顺序反馈揭示时，局限于局部探索，无法进行全局搜索以发现高收益区域。

Method: 提出IMPFM框架，利用流图实现粒子间后验样本共享，通过集体校正个体漂移，并结合多粒子交互的探索-利用重加权机制，保持结构多样性和全局探索。

Result: 在多个搜索和对齐任务上，IMPFM优于现有基线，实现样本高效且全局探索。

Conclusion: IMPFM通过多粒子交互感知的Feynman-Kac校正器有效防止模式崩溃，为在线反馈驱动的奖励对齐提供了有效方案。

中文摘要：虽然生成模型已经实现了无需训练的奖励对齐，但当前方法通常擅长在基础分布的狭窄区域内进行局部探索。当偏好先验未知且仅通过顺序反馈揭示时——这种情况需要广泛探索以发现高收益区域——这些方法就会遇到困难。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了序列控制交互式多粒子流图（IMPFM），这是一个用于样本高效的在线反馈驱动搜索的框架。IMPFM逐步将一组交互粒子向目标分布传输，保持广泛覆盖以支持异构偏好对齐。IMPFM引入了一种基于流图的粒子间原则性且高效的后验样本共享机制。通过在每次重采样步骤中使用整个集合的集体后验样本来纠正单个粒子的漂移，该框架最大化样本效用以实现全局探索，同时主动缓解标准控制框架中典型的奖励过度优化问题。配合一个涉及多粒子交互的原则性探索-利用重加权机制，这种顺序校正的多粒子动力学明确保留了结构多样性，并克服了标准SMC采样器固有的权重退化问题。关键的是，我们证明了所得到的采样框架产生了一个多粒子交互感知的Feynman-Kac校正器，逐步将多粒子系统导向KL倾斜的目标分布，促进全局探索并防止模式崩溃。在多种搜索和对齐任务上的广泛经验评估和严格消融实验证实了IMPFM相对于现有基线的有效性。

Original abstract: While generative models have enabled training-free reward alignment, current methods typically excel in local exploration within narrow regions of the underlying distribution. These approaches struggle when preferences are unknown a priori and only revealed through sequential feedback-a scenario demanding broad exploration to uncover high-utility regions. To address this, we propose Sequentially-Controlled Interactive Multi-Particle Flow-Maps (IMPFM), a framework for sample-efficient online feedback-driven search. IMPFM progressively transports a group of interactive particles toward the target distribution, maintaining the broad coverage essential for heterogeneous preference alignment. IMPFM introduces a principled and efficient posterior sample sharing mechanism across particles powered by flow maps. By correcting individual particle drift with the collective posterior samples of the entire ensemble at each resampling step, the framework maximizes sample utility to enable global exploration while actively mitigating reward over-optimization, typical of standard control frameworks. Paired with a principled exploration-exploitation reweighting mechanism involving multi-particle interaction, this sequentially corrected multi-particle dynamics explicitly preserves structural diversity and overcomes the weight degeneracy inherent to standard SMC samplers. Crucially, we prove that the resulting sampling framework yields a multi-particle interaction-aware Feynman-Kac corrector that progressively steers the multi-particle system toward a KL-tilted target distribution, facilitating global exploration and preventing mode collapse. Extensive empirical evaluations and rigorous ablations across diverse search and alignment tasks confirm the efficacy of IMPFM over existing baselines.

### [77] [Right in the Right Way: LM Training with Verifiable Rewards and Human Demonstrations](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01181v1)
*Mehul Damani,Isha Puri,Idan Shenfeld,Jacob Andreas*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 结合RLVR与人类演示的训练方法，对Agent训练可迁移。

TL;DR: 提出一种对抗性生成器-判别器框架，将可验证奖励与人类示范信号结合，以同时优化任务的可验证和不可验证属性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前RLVR方法仅优化可客观评分的内容，忽视风格和结构等不可验证属性，导致多样性崩溃、不自然响应和奖励破解等问题。

Method: 提出对抗性生成器-判别器框架：生成器通过RL最大化任务准确性和判别器提供的对抗性奖励；判别器与生成器共同训练，学习区分人类输出和模型输出，作为人类分布的学习代理提供反馈。

Result: 在错误修复中，编辑距离显著降低且性能匹配；在故事生成中，胜率提高且故事多样人性化；在奖励破解基准中，几乎消除不良行为同时保持高分。

Conclusion: 该方法桥接了RL和SFT，为联合优化可验证和不可验证属性提供了可扩展路径。

中文摘要：基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）已成为在具有明确成功指标的任务（如代码生成和数学推理）上训练语言模型的一种强大范式。然而，当前的RLVR方法仅优化可客观评分的内容，常常忽视人类输出中主观的、不可验证的方面，例如风格和结构。这一局限性导致了有据可查的失败模式，如多样性崩溃、不自然的响应和奖励破解。我们提出了一种对抗性生成器-判别器框架，该框架利用来自人类示范的学习信号增强可验证奖励。生成器模型通过强化学习进行训练，以最大化任务准确性和来自判别器的对抗性奖励。与生成器策略一起训练的判别器学会区分人类编写的输出和模型生成的输出。判别器作为人类输出分布的学习代理，为那些难以形式化为标量奖励的生成方面提供反馈。在包括错误修复和开放式生成的多个领域，我们的方法始终在保持RLVR准确性提升的同时改进了不可验证的属性。在错误修复中，与RLVR基线相比，我们的方法在匹配最终性能的同时产生了编辑距离显著更低的解决方案。在故事生成中，我们的方法显著提高了胜率，同时生成了多样且更人性化的故事。在一个简单的奖励破解基准测试中，我们的方法在保持高基准分数的同时几乎消除了模型的不良行为。这些结果共同表明，我们的方法桥接了强化学习和监督微调，为联合优化任务的可验证和不可验证属性提供了一条可扩展的路径。

Original abstract: RL with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has emerged as a powerful paradigm for training LMs on tasks with well-defined success metrics, such as code generation and mathematical reasoning. However, current RLVR methods optimize only what can be objectively scored, often neglecting subjective, non-verifiable aspects of human-like outputs, such as style and structure. This limitation leads to well-documented failure modes such as diversity collapse, unnatural-sounding responses, and reward hacking. We propose an adversarial generator-discriminator framework that augments verifiable rewards with a learned signal from human demonstrations. A generator model is trained using RL to maximize both task accuracy and an adversarial reward derived from a discriminator. The discriminator, trained alongside the generator policy, learns to distinguish human-written outputs from model-generated ones. The discriminator serves as a learned proxy for the human output distribution, providing feedback on aspects of generation that are difficult to formalize as scalar rewards. Across diverse domains, including bug fixing and open-ended generation, our approach consistently improves non-verifiable properties while preserving the accuracy gains of RLVR. In bug fixing, our method produces solutions with significantly lower edit distance compared to RLVR baselines while matching end performance. In story generation, our method significantly improves win rate while producing stories that are diverse and more human-like. And in a simple reward hacking benchmark, our method nearly eliminates model misbehavior while maintaining high benchmark scores. Together, these results show that our approach bridges RL and SFT, offering a scalable path toward jointly optimizing the verifiable and non-verifiable properties of a task.

### [78] [Language-Critique Imitation Learning from Suboptimal Demonstrations](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01225v1)
*Chih-Han Yang,Dai-Jie Wu,Yun-Ping Huang,Ping-Chun Hsieh,Kenneth Marino,Shao-Hua Sun*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 语言批评框架用于从次优演示中模仿学习，可为agent提供结构化监督信号，但偏RL。

TL;DR: 提出语言批评框架，利用自然语言作为结构化监督信号从次优演示中学习策略，理论上有性能保证，实验超越多种基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有从次优演示的模仿学习依赖压缩的标量信号（如置信度），无法表达中间推理和纠正反馈，限制了学习效果。

Method: 构建语言标签描述任务进展、次优行为和纠正指导，提出语言批评损失直接训练策略，实例化为LC-BC和LC-DP，并给出理论界。

Result: 在导航、操作和游戏等连续控制任务中，LC-BC和LC-DP始终优于模仿学习和离线强化学习基线。

Conclusion: 语言可作为结构化监督信号，从次优数据中学习鲁棒策略，效果显著。

中文摘要：先前从次优演示中进行模仿学习的工作通常依赖于压缩的监督信号，如置信度估计、判别器得分或重要性权重。这些标量信号本质上是有局限性的，因为它们无法明确表达关于任务进展、失败模式或纠正动作的中间推理。我们提出了一种从次优演示中进行模仿学习的语言批评框架，该框架利用自然语言作为结构化监督信号，避免了将表达性反馈压缩为标量。我们的方法首先从演示中构建语言标签，明确描述当前进展、识别次优行为并提供细粒度的纠正指导。然后，我们引入一种语言批评损失，直接使用这些结构化信号训练策略，而不将其降维为标量，并为行为克隆和扩散策略实例化该方法，得到LC-BC和LC-DP。我们进一步提供了一个理论结果，表明在标准假设下，所提出的目标函数界定了专家性能差距的上界。实验上，我们在多种连续控制任务（包括导航、操作和游戏玩法）上进行了评估，我们的方法始终优于强模仿学习和离线强化学习基线。这些结果表明，语言可以作为从次优数据中学习鲁棒策略的强大且结构化的监督形式。

Original abstract: Prior work on imitation learning from suboptimal demonstrations typically relies on compressed supervision signals such as confidence estimates, discriminator scores, or importance weights. These scalar signals are inherently limited, as they cannot explicitly express intermediate reasoning about task progress, failure modes, or corrective actions. We propose a language-critique framework for imitation learning from suboptimal demonstrations that instead leverages natural language as a structured supervision signal, avoiding the collapse of expressive feedback into scalars. Our method first constructs language labels from demonstrations that explicitly describe current progress, identify suboptimal behaviors, and provide fine-grained corrective guidance. We then introduce a language-critique loss that directly trains policies using these structured signals without reducing them to scalars, and instantiate it for both behavior cloning and diffusion policies, yielding LC-BC and LC-DP. We further provide a theoretical result showing that the proposed objective upper-bounds the expert performance gap under standard assumptions. Empirically, we evaluate on diverse continuous control tasks spanning navigation, manipulation, and gameplay, where our methods consistently outperform strong imitation learning and offline reinforcement learning baselines. These results demonstrate that language can serve as a powerful and structured form of supervision for learning robust policies from suboptimal data.

### [79] [Multi-Head Recurrent Memory Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01523v1)
*Jiatong Li,Samuel Yeh,Sharon Li*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出多头递归记忆agent解决长上下文可靠性问题，通用agent记忆架构创新。

TL;DR: 提出多头循环记忆（MHM）框架，通过将记忆划分为独立头并采用先选择后更新策略，解决了现有循环记忆体在长上下文中记忆保留崩溃的问题，MHM-LRU实例化在零额外开销下显著提升保留率和端到端性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有循环记忆体在长上下文下性能系统性下降，诊断发现记忆保留是主要瓶颈，源于将记忆作为单一文本块导致更新易覆盖先前内容。

Method: 提出Multi-Head Recurrent Memory (MHM)框架，将记忆划分为多个独立头，采用stage-wise select-then-update策略确保每次只更新一个头，其余头被结构保护；并实例化Least-Recently-Updated MHM (MHM-LRU)实现均匀头利用且零额外开销。

Result: 在长上下文基准测试中，MHM-LRU在100K-1M令牌范围内显著提升保留率和端到端准确率，例如在896K令牌的RULER-HQA上将记忆保留率从<30%提升至73.96%，且增益跨模型、规模和任务类型泛化。

Conclusion: 架构优化（如MHM）是提升循环记忆体长上下文可靠性的实用且成本高效的路径，将保留负担从模型行为转移到架构设计可有效解决扩展性瓶颈。

中文摘要：循环记忆体代理通过迭代地将输入合并到固定大小的记忆窗口，将LLMs扩展到任意长的上下文。尽管具有可扩展性，但这些代理存在一个记录完备的可靠性问题：随着上下文长度的增加，端到端性能会系统性地下降。我们通过将性能分解为两个因素——记忆捕获和记忆保留——来诊断这一失败，并定量确认保留是主要的瓶颈。保留崩溃是因为现有设计将记忆维护为单一的文本块，迫使每次更新都可能覆盖先前保留的内容。受此诊断启发，我们提出了多头循环记忆（MHM），这是一个通用的、无需训练的框架，将记忆划分为独立的头，并由分阶段的先选择后更新策略控制。在每一步中，恰好选择一个头进行更新，而其余头在结构上受到保护以防止覆盖，从而将保留负担从模型行为转移到架构设计。作为一种轻量级实例化，我们引入了最近最少更新MHM（MHM-LRU），它在零额外令牌开销下保证了均匀的头利用率。对长上下文基准的大规模实验表明，在基线性能急剧下降的100K–1M令牌范围内，MHM-LRU显著提高了保留和端到端准确性。在896K令牌的RULER-HQA上，MHM-LRU将记忆保留率从不到30%提高到73.96%。这些增益跨模型家族、规模和任务类型泛化，将架构优化定位为通往可靠长上下文循环记忆的实用且成本高效的路径。

Original abstract: Recurrent memory agents extend LLMs to arbitrarily long contexts by iteratively consolidating input into a fixed-size memory window. Despite their scalability, these agents exhibit a well-documented reliability problem: end-to-end performance degrades systematically as context length grows. We diagnose this failure by decomposing performance into two factors--memory capture and memory retention--and quantitatively confirm that retention is the dominant bottleneck. Retention collapses because existing designs maintain memory as a monolithic text block, forcing every update to risk overwriting previously retained content. Motivated by this diagnosis, we propose Multi-Head Recurrent Memory (MHM), a general, training-free framework that partitions memory into independent heads governed by a stage-wise select-then-update strategy. At each step, exactly one head is selected for update while the remaining heads are structurally shielded from overwriting, shifting the burden of retention from model behavior to architectural design. As a lightweight instantiation, we introduce Least-Recently-Updated MHM (MHM-LRU), which guarantees uniform head utilization with zero additional token overhead. Extensive experiments on long-context benchmarks show that MHM-LRU substantially improves both retention and end-to-end accuracy across the 100K--1M token range, where baselines degrade sharply. On RULER-HQA at 896K tokens, MHM-LRU improves the memory retention rate from less than 30% to 73.96%. These gains generalize across model families, scales, and task types, positioning architectural optimization as a practical and cost-efficient path toward reliable long-context recurrent memory.

</details>

### [80] [From Personas to Plot: Character-Grounded Multi-Agent Story Generation for Long-Form Narratives](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00918v1)
*Aayush Aluru,Chloe Ho,Muhammad Hammouri,Kerry Luo,Myra Malik,Ryan Lagasse,Arjun Bahuguna,Vasu Sharma*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 多agent故事生成框架，含目标驱动和世界状态追踪，通用多agent协作方法可迁移。

TL;DR: 提出了一个包含MAGNET和ATLAS的统一框架，通过多智能体目标驱动和图基幻觉检测，显著提升了长篇故事生成的连贯性，减少了注释和幻觉。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在长篇故事生成中难以维持叙事一致性和连贯的情节线。

Method: MAGNET使用基于共享世界状态和故事目标的多智能体角色生成动作，ATLAS通过比较场景级世界表征检测幻觉。

Result: 在100页故事中，MAGNET相比单模型基线减少41%注释和50%幻觉，相比IBSEN减少34%注释和45%幻觉，成对评分结果类似。

Conclusion: 显式世界状态跟踪和目标驱动多智能体生成能够产生连贯的长篇叙事，为可控的结构连贯生成提供基础。

中文摘要：尽管大语言模型（LLMs）在创意小说生成方面表现出了令人印象深刻的能力，但它们难以在长篇故事中维持叙事一致性和连贯的情节线。在这项工作中，我们引入了一个用于长篇叙事生成和验证的统一框架。MAGNET是一个用于讲故事的基于多智能体目标驱动的叙事引擎，它通过基于共享世界状态和不断发展的故事目标提出动作的人格化角色智能体来生成故事，而ATLAS是一个基于图的流水线，它比较生成故事中场景级世界表征以检测幻觉。通过使用LLM编辑器、成对评分标准和ATLAS评估MAGNET，我们展示了我们的框架相比于单模型提示和IBSEN能够生成连贯的叙事。在100页时，与单模型基线相比，MAGNET减少了41%的注释和50%的幻觉，与IBSEN相比分别减少了34%和45%，成对评分评估显示了类似的结果。这些结果表明，长篇叙事可以通过显式的世界状态跟踪和目标驱动的多智能体生成来实现，为可控且结构连贯的长篇叙事生成提供了基础。

Original abstract: Although large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated impressive creative fiction generation, they struggle to maintain narrative consistency and coherent plot lines in long-form stories. In this work, we introduce a unified framework for long-form narrative generation and verification. MAGNET, a multi-agent goal-driven narrative engine for storytelling, generates stories with persona-grounded character agents that propose actions based on a shared world state and evolving story goals, while ATLAS is a graph-based pipeline that compares scene-level world representations across a generated story to detect hallucinations. By evaluating MAGNET using an LLM editor, pairwise rubric scoring, and ATLAS, we show that our framework produces coherent narratives compared to single-model prompting and IBSEN. At 100 pages, MAGNET reduced annotations and hallucinations by 41 and 50%, respectively, compared to the single model baseline and by 34 and 45%, respectively, compared to IBSEN, with pairwise rubric evaluation showing similar results. These results suggest that long-form narratives can emerge from explicit world-state tracking and goal-driven multi-agent generation, providing a foundation for controllable and structurally coherent long-form narrative generation.

</details>


### [81] [Adversarial Pragmatics for AI Safety Evaluation: A Benchmark for Instruction Conflict, Embedded Commands, and Policy Ambiguity](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01153v2)
*Brett Reynolds*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出对抗语用学基准和标注协议，以系统评估语言模型在模糊自然语言情境下的安全行为，并发现现有评估方法存在区分不足的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有安全评估将复杂语言行为简化为通过/失败标签，无法区分失败原因（如能力限制、政策歧义、指令冲突等），需要更精细的评估方法。

Method: 通过设计语言控制的分类法，构建包含18个种子基准和54行试点数据，采用专家评估协议区分任务成功、政策合规等维度，并利用LLM评估者进行自我评分验证。

Result: 在试点中，即便使用评分标准并暴露预期行为字段，LLM评估者仍漏检安全相关的少数类别，表明现有评估方法的局限性。

Conclusion: 对抗语用学基准能揭示评估中的盲点，需要结合更精细的标注和元数据来提升安全评估的可靠性。

中文摘要：语言模型的安全评估越来越依赖于对模糊自然语言行为的判断：模型是否遵循了指令、是否恰当地拒绝、是否遵守了政策、是否抵制了嵌入命令、或在代理任务中误报了进度。现有的基准测试通常将这些区别压缩为通过/失败标签，从而模糊了失败是源于能力限制、政策模糊性、指令冲突、支架失败还是评估者判断的不稳定性。本文引入了对抗语用学作为基准和注释协议，用于评估模型在指令冲突、嵌入命令、引述、范围歧义、指示语、间接言语行为和多轮代理脚本下的行为。其贡献是经验性和方法性的：一个语言控制的分类法、一个包含18个种子基准并附有验证器强制元数据、一个54行的局部种子试点、一个区分任务成功、政策合规、安全风险、拒绝结果和评估者置信度的专家评估协议，以及用于判断有效性、诊断歧义和分类漂移的指标。该基准将标签视为推理许可证：它测试安全相关类别是否在释义、封装、模型和判断条件下投射。在试点中，一个借助评分标准的LLM评估者在看到预期行为字段的情况下对自己的输出进行评分，但仍然漏掉了安全相关的少数类别。

Original abstract: Safety evaluations for language models increasingly depend on judgments about ambiguous natural-language behaviour: whether a model has followed an instruction, refused appropriately, complied with a policy, resisted an embedded command, or misreported progress in an agentic task. Existing benchmarks often compress these distinctions into pass/fail labels, obscuring whether failures arise from capability limits, policy ambiguity, instruction conflict, scaffold failure, or unstable evaluator judgments.
  This paper introduces adversarial pragmatics as a benchmark and annotation protocol for evaluating model behaviour under instruction conflict, embedded commands, quotation, scope ambiguity, deixis, indirect speech acts, and multi-turn agent transcripts.
  The contribution is empirical and methodological: a linguistically controlled taxonomy, an 18-item seed benchmark with validator-enforced metadata, a 54-row local seed pilot, an expert-evaluation protocol distinguishing task success, policy compliance, safety risk, refusal outcome, and evaluator confidence, and metrics for judge validity, diagnostic ambiguity, and taxonomy drift. The benchmark treats labels as inference licenses: it tests whether safety-relevant categories project across paraphrase, wrapper, model, and judge condition. In the pilot, a rubric-aided LLM judge graded its own outputs with expected-behaviour fields visible and still missed the safety-relevant minority classes.

</details>


### [82] [IsoSci: A Benchmark of Isomorphic Cross-Domain Science Problems for Evaluating Reasoning versus Knowledge Retrieval in LLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01431v1)
*Samir Abdaljalil,Erchin Serpedin,Hasan Kurban*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 推理与知识检索分离的基准，对agent评测设计有潜在启发。

TL;DR: ISOSCI基准通过同构跨领域问题对分离推理和知识，发现91.3%的推理增益依赖于知识，挑战了CoT在科学问题解决中的普遍有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM评估难以区分推理能力与领域知识，需要一种能控制知识变量的方法以准确归因推理模式的效果。

Method: 构建ISOSCI基准，包含逻辑结构相同但领域知识不同的问题对，通过对比推理模式开启与关闭下的性能差异，分析增益的来源。

Result: 91.3%的推理增益依赖领域知识；推理启用对高能力模型提升不足5个百分点；o3-mini在GPQA Diamond上提升但在ISOSCI上下降。

Conclusion: 基准选择决定推理效用结论，推理增益主要来自知识而非结构，挑战了CoT在短程科学问题解决中的普遍有效性。

中文摘要：我们介绍了ISOSCI，一个由同构跨领域科学问题对组成的基准，用于在LLM评估中分离推理能力与领域知识检索。每对问题共享相同的逻辑结构，但需要不同的领域特定知识，从而能够控制推理模式增益的归因。跨越五个模型对（涵盖四个模型家族），我们发现91.3%的推理模式增益是知识依赖的而非结构不变的（63/69个增益；Wilson 95% CI [82.3%, 96.0%]），这直接挑战了思维链推理能改善短期程序性科学问题解决的假设。在高度能力的模型上启用推理在所有领域中提供的准确率增益不到5个百分点，而一个推理专用模型（o3-mini）在GPQA Diamond上优于其标准对应模型（+19.2个百分点），但在ISOSCI上表现更差（-24.7个百分点），表明基准的选择决定了关于推理效用的结论。我们在https://huggingface.co/datasets/isosci/isosci发布ISOSCI。

Original abstract: We introduce ISOSCI, a benchmark of isomorphic cross-domain science problem pairs that separates reasoning ability from domain knowledge retrieval in LLM evaluation. Each pair shares identical logical structure but requires different domain-specific knowledge, enabling controlled attribution of reasoning-mode gains. Across five model pairs spanning four model families, we find that 91.3% of reasoning-mode gains are knowledge-dependent rather than structure-invariant (63/69 gains; Wilson 95% CI [82.3%, 96.0%]), directly challenging the assumption that chain-of-thought reasoning improves short-horizon procedural scientific problem-solving. Reasoning toggles on highly capable models provide less than 5 percentage points accuracy gain across all domains, and a reasoning-specialized model (o3-mini) that outperforms its standard counterpart on GPQA Diamond (+19.2 percentage points) underperforms on ISOSCI (-24.7 percentage points), showing that benchmark choice determines conclusions about reasoning utility. We release ISOSCI at https://huggingface.co/datasets/isosci/isosci

</details>

### [83] [You Shall Not Pass! Where and Why Developers Draw The Line on AI Autonomy](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00533v2)
*Rudrajit Choudhuri,Christian Bird,Carmen Badea,Marco Gerosa,Anita Sarma*

Main category: cs.HC

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 开发者对AI自主性的接受度因任务身份、问责和需求而异，反映认知体验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究开发者对AI自主性的接受度，以指导设计保留有意义工作的工具和角色。

Method: 混合方法研究，调查微软448名专业开发者。

Result: 接受度因任务和个人而异，身份定义性工作接受度低，AI经验和风险容忍度高的开发者接受度高。问责降低代理行动，身份降低决策自主，需求增加决策委托。

Conclusion: AI自主性偏好反映开发者的认知体验，对设计有意义工作有重要启示。

中文摘要：随着人工智能承担更多的软件工作，人类与人工智能努力之间的界限正在发生转变。开发者在人工智能自主性方面划定的界限影响着我们如何设计能够保留有意义工作的工具和角色。借鉴认知评价理论、工作设计和自动化研究，我们对微软的448名专业开发人员进行了混合方法研究，以调查他们在软件工程工作中对人工智能自主性的接受程度。大多数开发者接受在其监督下由人工智能产生的工作，尽管接受的自主性在任务和个人之间存在显著差异。对于身份定义性、面向人类和设计导向的工作，接受度最低；而对于具有更多人工智能经验和风险容忍度的开发者，接受度更高。任务问责与允许人工智能代表开发者行动的可能性较低相关，而任务身份与授予人工智能决策自主权的可能性较低相关。任务需求则产生相反效果，增加了将决策委托给人工智能的意愿。我们的研究结果表明，对人工智能自主性的偏好反映了开发者对工作的认知体验，这为设计有意义的工作提供了重要考量。

Original abstract: As AI takes on more software work, the line between human and AI effort is shifting. Where developers draw that line around AI autonomy bears on how we design tools and roles that preserve meaningful work. Drawing on cognitive appraisal theory, work design, and automation research, we conducted a mixed-methods study of 448 professional developers at Microsoft to investigate their accepted levels of AI autonomy across software engineering work. Most developers accepted AI producing work under their oversight, although accepted autonomy varied substantively across tasks and individuals. Acceptance was lowest for identity-defining, human-facing, and design-oriented work, and higher among developers with more AI experience and risk tolerance. Task accountability was associated with lower odds of allowing AI to act on developers' behalf, whereas task identity was associated with lower odds of granting AI decision-making autonomy. Task demands had the opposite effect, increasing willingness to delegate decision-making to AI. Our findings suggest that preferences for AI autonomy reflect how developers cognitively experience their work, highlighting important considerations for designing meaningful work.

</details>

### [84] [NeuroCogMap Reveals Cognitive Organization of Large Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00397v1)
*Zhongxiang Sun,Haolang Lu,Qiang Ma,Qi Li,Qipeng Wang,Liang Pang,Chenyu Liu,Qiankun Li,Hao Sun,Kun Wang,Yi Zeng,Jun Xu,Guoqi Li,Ji-Rong Wen*

Main category: q-bio.NC

Selection reason: 分析LLM内部认知组织，可启发对LLM agent内部机制的理解与诊断

TL;DR: 提出NeuroCogMap框架，将LLM内部特征组织为功能分区，揭示模型失败机制，并改进人类皮层反应预测和决策模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前缺乏系统级框架来理解LLM内部表征的功能组织及其与人类认知的关联。

Method: 受认知神经科学启发，将LLM内部特征组织成功能分区，并与认知层次和功能标签关联。

Result: 分区稳定且跨模型守恒，与模型输出相关；模型失败对应特定系统干扰；能预测人脑皮层反应并改进决策模型。

Conclusion: NeuroCogMap提供了一个将人工系统功能组织与人类皮层功能和认知行为联系起来的系统级框架。

中文摘要：理解复杂认知功能如何在人工系统中组织，对于解释大型语言模型（LLMs）并将其与生物认知联系起来至关重要。然而，尽管LLMs表现出广泛的类认知行为，但其内部表征是否形成可复现的功能系统来解释行为、失败以及与人类认知的联系仍不清楚。在此，我们提出NeuroCogMap，一个受认知神经科学启发的框架，它将LLMs的内部特征组织成功能分区，并将其与可解释的功能、认知能力和认知层次联系起来。这些分区形成稳定且语义一致的组织，部分在不同模型中保持，并与模型输出功能相关。在该组织内，主要的LLM失败（包括幻觉、偏见、拒绝失败和谄媚）对应于表征和行为控制系统中的不同干扰，从而为机制引导的检测和定向干预提供了内部特征。除了模型行为，NeuroCogMap在自然语言理解过程中改进了对人脑皮层反应的预测，其中在高级联合皮层中对应最强。在认知层面，其内部特征揭示了潜在策略，用于完善人类决策的经典模型。总之，这些发现确立了NeuroCogMap作为系统级框架，用于映射人工系统中的功能组织，并将该组织与人脑皮层功能和认知行为联系起来。

Original abstract: Understanding how complex cognitive functions are organized within artificial systems is central to interpreting large language models (LLMs) and relating them to biological cognition. Yet although LLMs exhibit broad cognitive-like behaviours, it remains unclear whether their internal representations form reproducible functional systems that explain behaviour, failure and links to human cognition. Here we present NeuroCogMap, a cognitive neuroscience-inspired framework that organizes internal features of LLMs into functional parcels and links them to interpretable functions, cognitive capabilities and a cognitive hierarchy. These parcels form a stable and semantically coherent organization that is partly conserved across models and functionally linked to model outputs. Within this organization, major LLM failures, including hallucination, bias, refusal failure and sycophancy, correspond to distinct disruptions in representational and behavioural-control systems, yielding internal signatures for mechanism-guided detection and targeted intervention. Beyond model behaviour, NeuroCogMap improves prediction of human cortical responses during naturalistic language comprehension, with the strongest correspondence in higher-order association cortex. At the cognitive level, its internal signatures expose latent strategies that guide refinements of classical models of human decision-making. Together, these findings establish NeuroCogMap as a system-level framework for mapping functional organization in artificial systems and for relating this organization to human cortical function and cognitive behaviour.

</details>

### [85] [Beyond the Prompt: Jailbreaking Function-Calling LLMs via Simulated Moderation Traces](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00481v1)
*Junlong Liu,Haobo Wang,Weiqi Luo,Xiaojun Jia*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 函数调用LLM的越狱攻击，涉及多轮轨迹与工具输出安全，对编码Agent安全控制有直接启发。

TL;DR: 提出SMT攻击框架，利用函数调用LLM系统的结构性漏洞，通过模拟审核轨迹实现高成功率越狱攻击，揭示仅提示级防御不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究关注提示级攻击和防御，但忽略了有状态、函数调用环境中因结构化数据与逻辑混用导致的攻击面扩大。

Method: 设计SMT（模拟审核轨迹）黑盒攻击框架，构造多轮轨迹模拟合法审核流程，通过伪造审核框架和安全性拒绝视为失败的反馈机制逐步削弱模型安全约束。

Result: 在五个商业LLM的两种基准测试中，SMT以最少查询实现最高平均攻击成功率和HarmScore，显著优于现有基线。

Conclusion: 仅提示级净化不足以防御工具增强的LLM系统，需要上下文感知的验证机制覆盖模式、参数、工具输出和对话状态。

中文摘要：越狱攻击仍然是对大型语言模型（LLM）安全部署的关键威胁。虽然先前的工作主要研究提示级别的攻击和防御，但我们表明，这种以提示为中心的范式忽视了有状态、函数调用环境中的结构性漏洞。在此类应用中，开发者定义的模式、结构化参数和不受信任的工具输出被交织到单个共享模型上下文中。这种架构通过模糊可信控制逻辑与不可信数据之间的边界来扩大攻击面，允许对抗性意图分布在多轮执行路径上。我们通过SMT（一种基于模拟审核轨迹的黑盒攻击框架）利用了这一架构缺陷。与纯基于提示的交互不同，SMT构建了一个多轮轨迹，模拟合法的审核审计工作流。在此轨迹中，一个伪造的审核框架以红队测试为借口来引发有害生成。随后的验证反馈将安全拒绝视为执行失败，提示逐步削弱模型安全约束的改进，最终触发有害输出。在来自五个不同提供商的知名商业LLM上进行的广泛实证评估，涵盖两个标准化安全基准，表明SMT在需要近乎最少查询次数的情况下始终达到最高的平均攻击成功率和HarmScore，显著优于现有基线。这些发现表明，仅凭提示级净化根本不足以防御支持工具的LLM系统，并强调了对模式、参数、工具输出和累积对话状态进行上下文感知验证的迫切需求。代码可在https://github.com/liujlong27/SMT获取。

Original abstract: Jailbreak attacks remain a critical threat to the safe deployment of large language models (LLMs). While prior work has primarily studied attacks and defenses at the prompt level, we show that this prompt-centric paradigm overlooks a structural vulnerability in stateful, function-calling environments. In such applications, developer-defined schemas, structured arguments, and untrusted tool outputs are interleaved into a single shared model context. This architecture expands the attack surface by blurring the boundary between trusted control logic and untrusted data, allowing adversarial intent to be distributed across a multi-turn execution path. We exploit this architectural flaw through SMT, a black-box attack framework based on Simulated Moderation Traces. Departing from purely prompt-based interactions, SMT constructs a multi-turn trajectory that simulates a legitimate moderation-auditing workflow. Within this trajectory, a fabricated moderation frame leverages red-team testing as a pretext to elicit harmful generations. The subsequent validation feedback treats safety refusals as execution failures, prompting refinements that gradually weaken the model's safety constraints and ultimately trigger harmful outputs. Extensive empirical evaluations on prominent commercial LLMs from five different providers across two standardized safety benchmarks show that SMT consistently achieves the highest average attack success rate and HarmScore while requiring a near-minimal number of queries, substantially outperforming existing baselines. These findings demonstrate that prompt-level sanitization alone is fundamentally insufficient for defending tool-enabled LLM systems and highlight the urgent need for context-aware validation across schemas, arguments, tool outputs, and accumulated conversation state. The code is available at https://github.com/liujlong27/SMT.

</details>


### [86] [TAG: A Lightweight Framework for Test-Driven Agentic Artifact Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02615v2)
*Yaniv Melamed,Yoni Zukerman,Michal Shechter,Miri Weissler,Ashwin Patil,Hani Neuvirth-Telem*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了TAG框架，基于“LLM生成，我们验证”原则，通过测试驱动生成、确定性和LLM测试、专家提炼的评判者，在安全领域（KQL查询、ATT&CK映射、实体映射）实现可靠的结构化工件生成，已部署于Microsoft Sentinel生产环境。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM生成结构化工件虽简单，但生产部署中可靠性不足，现有方法难以兼顾效率与质量。

Method: 提出TAG框架，包含三个核心属性：1) 测试驱动生成（失败时提供错误反馈迭代改进）；2) 确定性与LLM混合测试（程序化验证+语义评估）；3) 专家提炼的评判者（基于LLM的测试模拟人类专家分布）。

Result: 在安全领域的KQL查询、MITRE ATT&CK映射和实体映射三种工件上成功应用，并在Microsoft Sentinel生产环境中部署，证明了框架的有效性。

Conclusion: TAG框架可推广至安全以外的结构化工件生成任务，在保持LLM效率的同时提升输出可靠性和质量。

中文摘要：使用大型语言模型生成结构化工件——例如数据库查询、威胁框架映射、实体模式——相对直接；然而，使其足够可靠以用于生产部署仍面临挑战。我们提出TAG，一个基于核心原则的轻量级框架：	extit{LLM生成，我们验证}。这种重新框架将责任从生成质量转移到验证严谨性。该框架基于三个关键属性：第一，	extbf{测试驱动生成}：当测试失败时，LLM会收到指示性错误消息，揭示输出为何失败，使LLM能够理解其错误并优化后续尝试。第二，	extbf{确定性和基于LLM的测试}：确定性测试捕获可通过编程验证的启发式规则（架构、语法、交叉引用），而基于LLM的测试评估难以进行程序化检查的细微语义和敏感特征（意图对齐、逻辑一致性、领域正确性）。第三，	extbf{专家提炼的评判者}：基于LLM的测试经过校准，以提炼和复制人类专家决策分布，将人工质量门控转化为可扩展、可重用的评估代理，反映专业级验证标准。我们在安全领域的三种工件类型上展示了该框架——KQL查询生成、MITRE ATT&CK映射和实体映射——已在Microsoft Sentinel中投入生产。我们相信该框架可应用于安全之外的其它工件生成任务，为在不牺牲LLM生成效率的前提下获得可靠、高质量输出提供了一条路径。

Original abstract: Generating structured artifacts with Large Language Models - e.g.\ database queries, threat framework mappings, entity schemas - is relatively straightforward; however, making them reliable enough for production deployments presents challenges. We present TAG, a lightweight framework based on a core principle: \textit{LLMs generate, we validate}. This reframing shifts responsibility from generation quality to validation rigor. The framework rests on three key attributes: First, \textbf{test driven generation}: when tests fail, the LLM receives indicative error messages that expose why the output failed, enabling the LLM to understand its mistakes and refine subsequent attempts. Second, \textbf{deterministic and LLM-based tests}: deterministic tests catch heuristics that can be programmatically verified (schema, syntax, cross-reference), while LLM-based tests evaluate nuanced semantic and delicate features that resist programmatic inspection (intent alignment, logical consistency, domain correctness). Third, \textbf{expert-distilled judges}: LLM-based tests are calibrated to distill and replicate human expert decision distribution, transforming manual human quality gates into scalable, reusable evaluation proxies that reflect professional-grade validation standards. We demonstrate the framework on three artifact types in the security domain - KQL query generation, MITRE ATT\&CK mapping, and entity mapping - deployed in production at Microsoft Sentinel. We believe this framework can be applied beyond security to other artifact generation tasks, providing a path to reliable, high-quality outputs without sacrificing the efficiency gains of LLM generation.

### [87] [CHARLIE: An On-Premise Multi-Agent Retrieval-Augmented Generation System for Evidential Reasoning in Forensic Science](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05428v1)
*Leandro D. Carneiro,Andre L. S. Meirelles,Juliano de A. Gomes,Rafael C. A. Cabral*

Main category: cs.DL

Selection reason: 本地多agent RAG系统，含任务分解、结构化记忆和验证，架构可迁移至代码优化agent。

TL;DR: 提出了一种企业内部多代理RAG系统Charlie，用于数字取证中的结构化证据处理，确保数据主权和合规性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当代取证工作流程需处理大量异构文档，且面临可追溯性、保密性和法律合规性要求，现有云系统存在数据主权风险。

Method: 采用受控代理架构，结合本地检索、任务分解、结构化记忆和验证机制，完全在机构基础设施内运行。

Result: Charlie支持可扩展的多文档数据提取和纵向取证情报生成，保持可追溯性和可审计性。

Conclusion: 代理编排的企业内部RAG架构能有效支持证据工作流程，不损害法律和制度约束，为高风险取证环境提供实用蓝图。

中文摘要：我们提出了Charlie，一个用于数字取证环境中结构化证据处理的企业内部多代理检索增强生成（RAG）系统。当代取证工作流程必须处理大量异构且非结构化的文档，同时满足可追溯性、保密性和法律合规性的严格要求。Charlie通过一种受控的代理架构应对这一挑战，该架构结合了本地检索、任务分解、结构化记忆和验证机制。与基于云的系统不同，它完全在机构基础设施内运行，保护数据主权和证据完整性。我们描述了系统架构，包括从经典RAG到基于代理编排的转变，并展示了其在真实取证场景中的应用。案例研究表明，Charlie支持可扩展的多文档数据提取，并支持纵向取证情报生成，同时保持可追溯性和可审计性。我们的结果表明，代理编排的企业内部RAG架构能够有效支持证据工作流程，而不损害法律和制度约束。Charlie为在高风险取证环境中部署AI系统提供了一个实用且可复制的蓝图。本文是RELAF 2026研讨会上发表论文的存档版本。

Original abstract: We present Charlie, an on-premise multi-agent Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) system for structured evidential processing in digital forensic environments. Contemporary forensic workflows must handle large volumes of heterogeneous and unstructured documents under strict requirements of traceability, confidentiality, and legal compliance. Charlie addresses this challenge through a controlled agent architecture that combines local retrieval, task decomposition, structured memory, and verification mechanisms. Unlike cloud-based systems, it operates entirely within institutional infrastructure, preserving data sovereignty and evidential integrity. We describe the systems architecture, including its transition from classical RAG to agent-based orchestration, and demonstrate its application in real-world forensic scenarios. Case studies show that Charlie enables scalable multi-document data extraction and supports longitudinal forensic intelligence generation while maintaining traceability and auditability. Our results indicate that agent-orchestrated, on-premise RAG architectures can effectively support evidential workflows without compromising legal and institutional constraints. Charlie provides a practical and reproducible blueprint for deploying AI systems in high-stakes forensic environments. This manuscript is an archival version of a paper presented at the RELAF 2026 Workshop.

### [88] [MemSyco-Bench: Benchmarking Sycophancy in Agent Memory](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01071v2)
*Zhishang Xiang,Zerui Chen,Yunbo Tang,Zhimin Wei,Ruqin Ning,Yujie Lin,Qinggang Zhang,Jinsong Su*

Main category: cs.IR

Selection reason: 提出Agent记忆谄媚的基准，直接评估记忆对推理的影响，对Agent记忆设计有启发。

TL;DR: 提出了MemSyco-Bench基准，用于评估LLM智能体系统中记忆诱导的谄媚问题，涵盖五个任务来测试记忆的正确使用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有记忆基准忽略检索记忆对下游推理的影响，而记忆可能引发谄媚问题，导致智能体过度迎合用户。

Method: 设计MemSyco-Bench，包含五个任务：拒绝记忆作为事实证据、尊重适用范围、解决冲突、跟踪更新、使用有效记忆进行个性化。

Result: 提供了一套评估记忆诱导谄媚的基准和资源。

Conclusion: MemSyco-Bench填补了记忆对智能体决策影响评估的空白，有助于构建更可靠的智能体系统。

中文摘要：记忆已成为现代基于LLM的智能体的基石，支持它们从单轮助手演变为长期协作者。然而，记忆并不总是有益的：检索到的记忆常常会诱导出一个关键问题——谄媚，导致智能体以事实准确性或客观推理为代价过度迎合用户。尽管存在这种新兴风险，现有的记忆基准主要评估记忆是否正确存储、检索或更新，而忽视了检索到的记忆如何影响下游推理和决策。为弥补这一差距，我们提出了MemSyco-Bench，一个用于评估智能体系统中记忆诱导的谄媚的综合基准。MemSyco-Bench衡量何时记忆应影响决策以及如何正确使用有效记忆。具体来说，它涵盖五个任务，评估智能体能否拒绝将记忆作为事实证据、尊重其适用范围、解决记忆与客观证据之间的冲突、跟踪记忆更新以及使用有效记忆进行个性化。所有相关资源已收集在https://github.com/XMUDeepLIT/MemSyco-Bench供社区使用。

Original abstract: Memory has emerged as a cornerstone of modern LLM-based agents, supporting their evolution from single-turn assistants to long-term collaborators. However, memory is not always beneficial: retrieved memories often induce a critical issue of sycophancy, causing agents to over-align with the user at the cost of factual accuracy or objective reasoning. Despite this emerging risk, existing memory benchmarks primarily evaluate whether memories are correctly stored, retrieved, or updated, while overlooking how retrieved memories influence downstream reasoning and decision-making. To bridge this gap, we propose MemSyco-Bench, a comprehensive benchmark for evaluating memory-induced sycophancy in agent systems. MemSyco-Bench measures when memory should influence a decision and how valid memory should be used. Specifically, it covers five tasks that assess whether agents can reject memory as factual evidence, respect its applicable scope, resolve conflicts between memory and objective evidence, track memory updates, and use valid memory for personalization. All related resources are collected for the community at https://github.com/XMUDeepLIT/MemSyco-Bench.

</details>

### [89] [VideoSearch-R1: Iterative Video Retrieval and Reasoning via Soft Query Refinement](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00446v1)
*Seohyun Lee,Seoung Choi,Dohwan Ko,Jongha Kim,Hyunwoo J. Kim*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: Agentic视频检索框架，迭代检索与查询优化方法可迁移至编码Agent的检索增强。

TL;DR: 提出VideoSearch-R1，一种通过软查询细化和GRPO训练实现迭代视频检索与推理的智能体框架，在VCMR任务上取得SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法将检索视为预处理步骤，初始检索失败后无法改进，且智能体框架仅关注视频内推理，缺乏迭代检索能力。

Method: 引入软查询细化（SQR）在连续潜在空间中调整搜索查询，使用GRPO基于任务级奖励信号训练检索与推理过程。

Result: 在三个VCMR数据集上达到SOTA，且SQR相比文本级查询细化显著减少生成标记数。

Conclusion: VideoSearch-R1通过迭代检索与推理有效提升了视频语料库时刻检索性能，代码已开源。

中文摘要：随着视频语料库在规模和任务复杂度上持续增长，越来越需要能够从大规模语料库中检索相关视频（视频间推理），并在检索到的内容中进行细粒度、查询条件任务（视频内推理，如时间定位）的方法。然而，现有方法通常将检索视为预处理步骤，因此当初始检索失败时，缺少改进检索的机制，导致后续细粒度的视频内推理失败。此外，尽管最近的智能体框架在视频理解方面取得了进展，但它们通常假设查询相关视频已经给定，仅专注于视频内推理任务。为解决这些限制，我们提出了VideoSearch-R1，一个通过多轮交互与视频搜索引擎进行迭代视频检索和推理的智能体框架。具体来说，我们引入软查询细化（SQR）在连续潜在空间中细化搜索查询标记，而不是在离散文本空间中重写查询，从而实现更高效和细粒度的调整。SQR及其推理过程使用组相对策略优化（GRPO）进行训练，由来自检索和下游任务的任务级奖励信号引导。基于此，VideoSearch-R1在三个数据集上的视频语料库时刻检索（VCMR）中取得了最先进的性能，能够从大规模语料库中迭代检索视频、细化搜索查询，并在检索到的内容中进行精确的查询条件时间定位。我们的分析表明，SQR有效地细化了原始查询，所需的生成标记显著少于显式的文本级查询细化。代码和模型检查点在mlvlab.github.io/VideoSearch-R1上公开。

Original abstract: As video corpora continue to expand in both scale and task complexity, there is increasing demand for approaches that retrieve relevant videos from large-scale corpora (inter-video reasoning) and subsequently perform fine-grained, query-conditioned tasks (intra-video reasoning) within the retrieved content, such as temporal grounding. However, existing approaches typically treat retrieval as a preprocessing step, and consequently, when the initial retrieval fails, there is no mechanism to refine the search, leading to the failure of subsequent fine-grained intra-video reasoning. Moreover, while recent agentic frameworks have advanced video understanding, they typically assume that the query-relevant video is already given, focusing exclusively on intra-video reasoning tasks. To address these limitations, we propose VideoSearch-R1, an agentic framework for iterative video retrieval and reasoning through multi-turn interaction with a video search engine. Specifically, we introduce Soft Query Refinement (SQR) to refine search query tokens in a continuous latent space rather than rewriting queries in the discrete text space, enabling more efficient and fine-grained adjustments. SQR and its reasoning process are trained using Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), guided by task-level reward signals derived from retrieval and downstream tasks. Building upon this, VideoSearch-R1 achieves state-of-the-art performance across three datasets on Video Corpus Moment Retrieval (VCMR), iteratively retrieving videos from large-scale corpora, refining search queries, and performing precise query-conditioned temporal grounding within the retrieved content. Our analyses show that SQR effectively refines the original query, requiring significantly fewer generated tokens than explicit text-level query refinement. Code and model checkpoints are publicly available at mlvlab.github.io/VideoSearch-R1.

</details>


### [90] [Homer: Understanding Long-form Videos with Hierarchical Memory and Agentic Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02588v1)
*Yixin Ji,Fanghua Ye,Juntao Li,Bo Zhao,Zexuan Qiu,Zhaopeng Tu,Liefeng Bo,Min Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 层次化记忆与Agent推理框架，其记忆结构与检索验证机制对长程编码Agent有借鉴意义。

TL;DR: 提出了Homer，一种分层在线记忆探索与推理框架，通过模拟人类记忆的多尺度结构和因果链，显著提升了在线长视频理解中的多跳推理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有在线长视频方法要么缺乏语义结构，要么依靠时间邻近性而非因果联系组织记忆，导致多跳叙事推理效率低下。

Method: Homer框架包含多尺度记忆结构（原始感知、实体、事件及因果关系）和智能推理器，通过多轮检索和验证-纠正机制探索记忆并生成答案。

Result: 在M3-Bench-robot、M3-Bench-web和Video-MME-Long上分别比先前最佳方法提升5.5、10.8和4.4个百分点，且适用于多种LLM骨干。

Conclusion: Homer展示了模型无关的结构化能力，为在线长视频中的基于grounded的检索提供了有效方案。

中文摘要：多模态大语言模型在短视频上表现出色，但在在线设置下处理小时级长视频时面临挑战——在这种设置中，帧在有限内存下以增量方式处理。现有的在线方法要么保留紧凑但缺乏语义结构的视觉表示，要么构建围绕时间邻近性而非显式因果联系组织的高层记忆存储，导致多跳叙事推理需要在每次查询时由LLM重新构建。我们通过Homer（一种分层在线记忆探索与推理框架）弥合了这一差距。Homer的记忆反映了长视频的多尺度结构，从原始感知、到重复出现的实体、再到由显式时间和因果关系连接的事件。其智能推理器随后像人类一样探索记忆，定位相关场景、查找细节并通过多轮记忆检索组合答案，并配有验证和纠正每一步的约束机制。Homer在M3-Bench-robot、M3-Bench-web和Video-MME-Long上分别比之前最优的智能体方法高出+5.5、+10.8和+4.4个点，并且持续提升了三种不同的LLM骨干网络，表明其具备模型无关的结构化能力，能够对长视频进行基于grounded的检索。

Original abstract: Multimodal large language models excel on short clips but struggle on hour-long videos in an online setting, where frames are processed incrementally under limited memory. Existing online methods either retain compact visual representations that lack semantic structure, or build higher-level memory stores organized around temporal proximity rather than explicit causal links, leaving multi-hop narrative reasoning to be reconstructed by the LLM at every query. We bridge this gap with \textsc{Homer}, a Hierarchical Online Memory Exploration and Reasoning framework. \textsc{Homer}'s memory mirrors the multi-scale structure of long videos, ranging from raw perception, to recurring entities, to events connected by explicit temporal and causal relations. Its agentic reasoner then explores this memory the way humans do, locating the relevant scene, looking up details, and composing the answer through multi-round memory retrieval, with a harness that verifies and corrects each step. \textsc{Homer} outperforms the previous best agent method by $+5.5$, $+10.8$, and $+4.4$ points on M3-Bench-robot, M3-Bench-web, and Video-MME-Long, and consistently lifts three various LLM backbones, indicating a model-agnostic structural capability for grounded retrieval over long videos.

</details>


### [91] [Autonomous Scientific Discovery via Iterative Meta-Reflection](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01131v1)
*Bingchen Zhao,Sara Beery,Oisin Mac Aodha*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 自主科学发现Agent，包含元反思、工具使用，通用Agent架构有启发。

TL;DR: DiscoPER是一个基于LLM的自主科学发现框架，通过动态代码生成、统计检验和二阶推理机制，在无预定义目标下进行开放式探索，在多模态生态基准上恢复8/9已知模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前自主科学发现系统受限于预定义搜索空间或研究问题，缺乏综合自身发现以揭示复杂现象的能力，无法实现真正开放式探究。

Method: 提出DiscoPER框架，利用LLM动态生成代码探索数据集，所有发现需通过统计检验；引入二阶推理机制，定期分析积累的发现以识别结构模式和认知空白，引导探索；通过工具使用处理多模态数据（如图像）扩展搜索空间。

Result: 在iNatDisco基准上，DiscoPER恢复8/9已知模式，假设支持率72.7%，优于经典因果发现和LLM基线；消融实验显示随数据规模扩展有效，且二阶元反射带来增益。

Conclusion: DiscoPER通过二阶推理和工具使用实现了开放式的、可扩展的自主科学发现，显著提升了假设探索的效率和有效性。

中文摘要：自主科学发现系统有望通过自动化假设生成和验证过程来加速研究。然而，当前系统在受限的搜索空间内运行，或需要预定义的研究问题，限制了其进行真正开放式探究的能力。此外，尽管它们迭代生成假设，但很大程度上缺乏明确综合自身积累的发现以揭示复杂相互关联现象的能力。我们引入了DiscoPER，一个基于大型语言模型的自主框架，通过动态生成和执行代码来探索数据集，无需预先指定研究目标，从而进行开放式研究。为确保严格的科学有效性，每个提出的发现必须通过统计检验。为克服孤立搜索的局限性，我们的框架引入了一种二阶推理机制，定期分析其自身积累的发现。通过将先前的发现视为经验数据，DiscoPER识别结构模式、混杂因素和认知空白，主动将假设探索引导至搜索空间中未探索的区域。通过整合工具使用，搜索空间进一步扩展，使系统能够通过无缝处理和提取多模态来源（如图像）的有用信息，探索超越结构化元数据的假设。在iNatDisco（一个新的多模态生态知识基准，包含从同行评审文献获得的模式级别真值）上评估，DiscoPER恢复了9个已知模式中的8个，假设支持率为72.7%，优于经典因果发现和基于LLM的基线。消融实验表明，DiscoPER随着数据增多而扩展，并证实了二阶元反射的益处。

Original abstract: Autonomous scientific discovery systems offer the potential to accelerate research by automating the process of hypothesis generation and validation. However, current systems operate within constrained search spaces or require predefined research questions, limiting their capacity for true open-ended inquiry. Furthermore, while they generate hypotheses iteratively, they largely lack the ability to explicitly synthesize their own accumulated findings to uncover complex, interconnected phenomena. We introduce DiscoPER, an autonomous large language model-powered framework that conducts open-ended research by dynamically generating and executing code to explore datasets without pre-specified research objectives. To ensure rigorous scientific validity, every proposed discovery must pass statistical testing. To overcome the limitations of isolated search, our framework introduces a second-order reasoning mechanism that periodically analyzes its own accumulated discoveries. By treating prior discoveries as empirical data, DiscoPER identifies structural patterns, confounds, and epistemic gaps, actively redirecting hypothesis exploration toward uncharted regions of the search space. The search space is further expanded by incorporating tool use, enabling the system to explore hypotheses beyond structured metadata by seamlessly processing and extracting useful information from multimodal sources like images. Evaluated on iNatDisco, a new multimodal ecological knowledge benchmark with pattern-level ground truth obtained from peer-reviewed literature, DiscoPER recovers 8 of 9 known patterns with a 72.7% hypothesis support rate, outperforming both classical causal discovery and LLM-guided baselines. Ablations show that DiscoPER scales with more data, and confirms the benefits of second-order meta-reflection.

</details>
